      ctx.lineWidth = lerp(1.8, 1.0, t);
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(xl, y);
      ctx.lineTo(xr, y);
      ctx.stroke();
    }

    // side glow edges
    ctx.lineWidth = 3.2;
    ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr([78,239,255], 0.22*alpha);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x1t, topY); ctx.lineTo(x1b, botY); ctx.stroke();
    ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr([255,84,214], 0.18*alpha);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x2t, topY); ctx.lineTo(x2b, botY); ctx.stroke();

    // haze
    const haze = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, botY*0.78, 0, cx, botY*0.78, Math.min(W,H)*0.75);
    haze.addColorStop(0, `rgba(255,255,255,${0.12*alpha})`);
    haze.addColorStop(1, `rgba(255,255,255,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle = haze;
    ctx.fillRect(0, topY, W, botY-topY);

    ctx.restore();

    // subtle "hole" feel
    const holeR = Math.min(W,H)*0.20;
    const hole = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, topY, 0, cx, topY, holeR);
    hole.addColorStop(0, `rgba(20,18,28,${0.62*alpha})`);
    hole.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle = hole;
    ctx.fillRect(cx-holeR, topY-holeR, holeR*2, holeR*2);
  }

  function drawSun(x,y,r,color, glow=1, alpha=1){
    const R = r*(7*glow);
    const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
    g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(color, 0.24*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(0.22, rgbStr(lighten(color,0.10), 0.14*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(color, 0.97*alpha); ctx.fill();

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x-r*0.22,y-r*0.22,r*0.35,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${0.35*alpha})`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // ---------- Space ----------
  function drawSpace(alpha=1){
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(5,6,12,${alpha})`; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const neb=ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.35,H*0.35,0, W*0.35,H*0.35, Math.min(W,H)*0.9);
    neb.addColorStop(0, `rgba(120,90,255,${0.10*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(0.5, `rgba(80,220,255,${0.05*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=neb; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    for(let i=0;i<140;i++){
      const x=(hash2(i,9.1)*W), y=(hash2(i,2.7)*H);
      const a=(hash2(i,6.3)*0.06+0.01)*alpha;
      const r=hash2(i,4.2)*1.2+0.2;
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }

    for(const s of stars){
      const x=s.x*W, y=s.y*H;
      const tw=(Math.sin(time*1.6+s.twSeed)*0.5+0.5);
      const a=lerp(0.35,0.95,tw)*alpha;

      const R=s.r*10;
      const g=ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
      g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(s.color, 0.24*a));
      g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
      ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

      ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(s.color,a);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,s.r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }
  }

  // ---------- Update / Render ----------
  function update(dt){
    time += dt;

    // zoom inertia
    zoomVel *= 0.84;
    zoom = clamp(zoom - zoomVel, 0, 1);

    // 明顯時間變色（你要明顯）
    timeDay = (timeDay + dt*0.05) % 1;
    const sky = skyAt(timeDay);

    const inTerrain = (zoom > 0.45);
    const wantsMove = pointer.down && !inColorize && inTerrain;

    // travel only when holding
    const targetVel = wantsMove ? 1 : 0;
    travelVel += (targetVel - travelVel) * (1 - Math.pow(0.001, dt));
    travel += travelVel * dt * 1.55;

    // approach / reach
    if(!inColorize){
      if(wantsMove) reach -= dt*0.62;
      else          reach += dt*0.08;
      reach = clamp(reach,0,1);

      if(reach <= 0.04){
        inColorize=true;
        colorizeT=0;
        pendingColor=randomDreamColor();
      }
    } else {
      colorizeT += dt*1.15;
      if(colorizeT >= 1){
        addStar(pendingColor);
        sun.curColor = sun.baseColor.slice();
        inColorize=false;
        reach=1;
      } else {
        const t=colorizeT;
        const up = t<0.55 ? smooth(t/0.55) : smooth((1-t)/0.45);
        sun.curColor = mixRGB(sun.baseColor, pendingColor, up);
      }
    }

    render(sky, wantsMove);
  }

  function render(sky, wantsMove){
    const layer=currentLayer();
    const terrainAlpha = clamp((zoom - 0.35)/0.65, 0, 1);
    const spaceAlpha = 1 - terrainAlpha;

    if(spaceAlpha>0.001) drawSpace(spaceAlpha);

    if(terrainAlpha>0.001){
      const flow = travel*2.45;

      // NEW: topo dream terrain
      drawTerrainTopoSolid(sky, flow, terrainAlpha);

      const sunX = W*(sun.x + Math.sin(time*0.20)*0.002);
      const sunY = H*(sun.y + Math.cos(time*0.16)*0.002);

      // corridor (match dream palette)
      drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, travel, travelVel, sky, terrainAlpha);

      // approach => sun grows
      const baseR = Math.min(W,H)*0.018;
      const grow = lerp(1.0, 3.0, smooth(1-reach));
      const pulse = (Math.sin(time*1.2)*0.5+0.5);
      const glow  = lerp(1.0, 2.0, smooth(1-reach));
      drawSun(sunX, sunY, baseR*grow*(1.0+pulse*0.05), sun.curColor, glow, terrainAlpha);

      // hint
      if(!pointer.down && !inColorize){
        const a=(Math.sin(time*2.0)*0.5+0.5)*0.35*terrainAlpha;
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
        ctx.font=`600 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.018))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
        ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
        ctx.fillText('按住左鍵追光前進', W*0.5, H*0.82);
      }

      // layer2 overlay
      if(inColorize){
        const t=smooth(colorizeT);
        const flashA = lerp(0.00,0.28, Math.sin(Math.PI*t));
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${flashA*terrainAlpha})`;
        ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

        const ringR = lerp(baseR*2.2, Math.min(W,H)*0.36, t);
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(sunX,sunY,ringR,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(pendingColor, 0.46*terrainAlpha);
        ctx.lineWidth = lerp(2.6,1.0,t);
        ctx.stroke();

        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${0.62*terrainAlpha})`;
        ctx.font=`500 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.016))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
        ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
        ctx.fillText('染色中… 成為宇宙的一顆星', W*0.5, H*0.90);
      }
    }

    // HUD
    pillLayer.textContent = `layer: ${inColorize ? '2' : layer}`;
    pillStars.textContent = `stars: ${stars.length}`;
    pillZoom.textContent  = `zoom: ${zoom.toFixed(2)}`;
    pillTime.textContent  = `time: ${Math.round(timeDay*100)}%`;

    // space hint
    if(layer===3 && !inColorize){
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.55)`;
      ctx.font=`500 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.016))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
      ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
      ctx.fillText('滾輪放大回到地勢圖（第一層）', W*0.5, H*0.90);
      if(stars.length===0){
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.42)`;
        ctx.fillText('宇宙尚未生成繁星：先回去追光並完成染色', W*0.5, H*0.84);
      }
    }
  }

  // ---------- Loop ----------
  let last=performance.now();
  function loop(now){
    const dt=Math.min(0.033,(now-last)/1000);
    last=now;
    update(dt);
    requestAnimationFrame(loop);
  }
  requestAnimationFrame(loop);
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>

如果你覺得還差一點「更像地勢圖」的關鍵，我下一步可以再加兩個效果（你不用回答也行，我直接做也可以）：

更硬的色塊分層（像印刷地勢圖那樣一層一層完全不漸層）

等高線變成 “多重密線”（每層加細線＋粗主等高線）

你想先把哪個加強？（我傾向先做 2，因為一加就很像地勢圖。）



你說：
已上傳一個圖像
現在山河沒有高低起伏，中間的光點也不見了
背景的日夜更替也不見了。


ChatGPT 說：

懂，你這三個症狀其實是同一類問題：渲染順序／顏色覆蓋把地形「壓平」了、通道把中心蓋住了、天空的時間色被稀釋到看不出來。

我直接給你一份「修好版」：

✅ 地勢起伏變明顯（高度振幅加大＋近景厚度加大＋輪廓線更清楚）

✅ 中間光點一定看得到（最後一層再畫一次，永遠在最上層）

✅ 日夜更替超明顯（天空色變＋暗角＋夜晚星塵出現，變化肉眼很清楚）

✅ 通道保留「往洞口/太陽」方向感，但不會蓋掉山河與光點

把你目前的 html 整份覆蓋成下面這份（單檔可跑）：

HTML
<!doctype html>
<html lang="zh-Hant">
<head>
  <meta charset="utf-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" />
  <title>三層空間｜互動響應式</title>
  <style>
    :root{ --fg: rgba(255,255,255,.9); --muted: rgba(255,255,255,.62); }
    html,body{height:100%;margin:0;background:#05060c;overflow:hidden;font-family:ui-sans-serif,system-ui,-apple-system,"Segoe UI",Arial;}
    #wrap{position:fixed;inset:0;}
    canvas{position:absolute;inset:0;width:100%;height:100%;}
    .hud{
      position:fixed;left:16px;top:14px;z-index:10;
      color:var(--fg);font-size:12px;line-height:1.5;
      user-select:none;pointer-events:none;
      padding:10px 12px;border-radius:14px;
      border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.12);
      background:rgba(0,0,0,.22);
      backdrop-filter: blur(6px);
      max-width:min(600px, calc(100vw - 32px));
    }
    .hud .muted{color:var(--muted)}
    .pillrow{display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap;margin-top:8px}
    .pill{
      padding:5px 10px;border-radius:999px;
      border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.12);
      background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);
      color:var(--muted);
    }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div id="wrap"><canvas id="c"></canvas></div>

  <div class="hud">
    <div><b>操作</b>：左鍵按住前進｜放開停止｜滾輪縮小進宇宙｜滾輪放大回地勢</div>
    <div class="muted">抵達亮點 → 自動染色 → 記錄成宇宙繁星（第三層）。</div>
    <div class="pillrow">
      <div class="pill" id="pillLayer">layer: 1</div>
      <div class="pill" id="pillStars">stars: 0</div>
      <div class="pill" id="pillZoom">zoom: 1.00</div>
      <div class="pill" id="pillTime">time: 0%</div>
    </div>
  </div>

<script>
(() => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('c');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', { alpha:false });

  const pillLayer = document.getElementById('pillLayer');
  const pillStars = document.getElementById('pillStars');
  const pillZoom  = document.getElementById('pillZoom');
  const pillTime  = document.getElementById('pillTime');

  // ---------- Responsive ----------
  let W=0,H=0,dpr=1;
  function resize(){
    dpr = Math.max(1, Math.min(2, window.devicePixelRatio || 1));
    W = Math.floor(window.innerWidth);
    H = Math.floor(window.innerHeight);
    canvas.width = Math.floor(W*dpr);
    canvas.height= Math.floor(H*dpr);
    canvas.style.width = W+'px';
    canvas.style.height= H+'px';
    ctx.setTransform(dpr,0,0,dpr,0,0);
  }
  window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
  resize();

  // ---------- Utils ----------
  const clamp=(v,a,b)=>Math.max(a,Math.min(b,v));
  const lerp=(a,b,t)=>a+(b-a)*t;
  const smooth=(t)=>t*t*(3-2*t);
  const fract=(x)=>x-Math.floor(x);

  function hash2(x,y){
    const s = Math.sin(x*127.1 + y*311.7) * 43758.5453123;
    return fract(s);
  }
  function valueNoise(x,y){
    const xi=Math.floor(x), yi=Math.floor(y);
    const xf=x-xi, yf=y-yi;
    const a=hash2(xi,yi), b=hash2(xi+1,yi);
    const c=hash2(xi,yi+1), d=hash2(xi+1,yi+1);
    const u=smooth(xf), v=smooth(yf);
    return lerp(lerp(a,b,u), lerp(c,d,u), v);
  }
  function fbm(x,y){
    let f=0, amp=0.62, freq=1.0;
    for(let i=0;i<5;i++){
      f += amp * valueNoise(x*freq, y*freq);
      freq *= 2.0;
      amp *= 0.52;
    }
    return f;
  }
  function mixRGB(a,b,t){
    return [
      Math.round(lerp(a[0],b[0],t)),
      Math.round(lerp(a[1],b[1],t)),
      Math.round(lerp(a[2],b[2],t)),
    ];
  }
  function rgbStr(c,a=1){ return `rgba(${c[0]},${c[1]},${c[2]},${a})`; }
  function darken(c,t){ return mixRGB(c,[0,0,0],t); }
  function lighten(c,t){ return mixRGB(c,[255,255,255],t); }

  // ---------- Input ----------
  const pointer = {x:0,y:0,down:false};
  window.addEventListener('pointerdown',(e)=>{ if(e.button!==0) return; pointer.down=true; pointer.x=e.clientX; pointer.y=e.clientY; });
  window.addEventListener('pointerup',(e)=>{ if(e.button!==0) return; pointer.down=false; });
  window.addEventListener('pointermove',(e)=>{ pointer.x=e.clientX; pointer.y=e.clientY; });

  let zoom=1.0, zoomVel=0;
  window.addEventListener('wheel',(e)=>{
    e.preventDefault?.();
    zoomVel += Math.sign(e.deltaY) * 0.06;
  }, {passive:false});

  // ---------- State ----------
  let time=0;
  let timeDay=0;        // 0..1 (循環)
  let travel=0;
  let travelVel=0;
  let reach=1;

  let inColorize=false;
  let colorizeT=0;
  let pendingColor=[255,140,220];

  const sun={ x:0.5, y:0.44, baseColor:[255,246,222], curColor:[255,246,222] };

  const stars=[];
  function addStar(color){
    const cx=sun.x+(Math.random()-0.5)*0.12;
    const cy=sun.y+(Math.random()-0.5)*0.12;
    stars.push({ x:clamp(cx,0.06,0.94), y:clamp(cy,0.06,0.94), r:lerp(0.9,2.8,Math.random()), color, twSeed:Math.random()*1000 });
  }

  // ---------- Sky (日夜更替要超明顯) ----------
  const skyStops=[
    {t:0.00, c:[252,252,255]},  // 白
    {t:0.33, c:[255,214,195]},  // 暖承載
    {t:0.66, c:[34, 86, 195]},  // 深藍
    {t:1.00, c:[10, 12, 20]},   // 黑灰
  ];
  function skyAt(t){
    t=clamp(t,0,1);
    for(let i=0;i<skyStops.length-1;i++){
      const a=skyStops[i], b=skyStops[i+1];
      if(t>=a.t && t<=b.t){
        const u=smooth((t-a.t)/(b.t-a.t));
        return mixRGB(a.c,b.c,u);
      }
    }
    return skyStops[skyStops.length-1].c;
  }
  function nightAmount(t){ // 0白天 -> 1夜晚
    // t>0.62 之後快速進夜
    const n = clamp((t-0.58)/0.25, 0, 1);
    return smooth(n);
  }

  function currentLayer(){ return (zoom<0.45)?3:1; }

  function randomDreamColor(){
    const choices=[[255,80,200],[80,240,255],[255,230,80],[170,120,255],[120,255,170],[255,140,110]];
    const a=choices[(Math.random()*choices.length)|0];
    const b=choices[(Math.random()*choices.length)|0];
    return mixRGB(a,b,Math.random()*0.85);
  }

  // ---------- Dream topo palette ----------
  const topoPalette = [
    [255, 84, 214],
    [ 78, 239, 255],
    [255, 230,  92],
    [168, 120, 255],
    [120, 255, 176],
    [255, 160, 120],
  ];
  function topoColor(h01, sky){
    // 更硬的分層（地勢圖感）
    const levels = 9;
    const q = Math.floor(clamp(h01,0,1)*levels)/levels;

    const idx = Math.floor(q * (topoPalette.length-1));
    const u = (q*(topoPalette.length-1)) - idx;
    const c = mixRGB(topoPalette[idx], topoPalette[Math.min(idx+1, topoPalette.length-1)], smooth(u));

    // 仍保留少量時間色氣氛
    return mixRGB(c, sky, 0.10);
  }

  // ---------- Layer 1: terrain with REAL relief ----------
  function drawTerrainTopoSolid(sky, flow, alpha=1){
    // SKY (強對比)
    const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
    g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(lighten(sky,0.10), alpha));
    g.addColorStop(0.55, rgbStr(sky, alpha));
    g.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(darken(sky,0.32), alpha));
    ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    // 夜晚加星塵（讓日夜更替「看得見」）
    const night = nightAmount(timeDay);
    if(night > 0.02){
      for(let i=0;i<180;i++){
        const x = hash2(i, 9.1)*W;
        const y = hash2(i, 2.7)*H*0.62;
        const a = (hash2(i, 6.3)*0.10 + 0.02) * night * alpha;
        const r = hash2(i, 4.2)*1.3 + 0.2;
        ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
      }
    }

    const horizon = H*0.17;
    const depthEnd = H*0.96;

    const strips = 100;
    const stepX = Math.max(6, Math.floor(W/190));

    for(let i=0;i<strips;i++){
      const z = i/(strips-1);          // 0遠 -> 1近
      const yBase = lerp(horizon, depthEnd, z);

      // 強化前進感：近景 sampling 速度更快
      const speed = lerp(0.10, 2.10, z);
      const ny = z*2.9 + flow*0.22*speed;

      const persp = lerp(0.14, 1.38, z);

      // ✅ 你要的「高低起伏」：這裡振幅加大（比之前大很多）
      const ampTop = lerp(18, 130, z);

      const freq = lerp(0.0065, 0.00175, z);

      const top=[];
      let hAvg=0, hN=0;

      for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
        const nx = (x - W*0.5) * freq * persp;
        const n  = fbm(nx + 12, ny + 4);
        const n2 = fbm(nx*1.55 + 40, ny*0.92 + 1.2);
        const h = (n*0.68 + n2*0.32 - 0.5);
        const yy = yBase + h*ampTop;
        top.push([x,yy]);

        const h01 = clamp(h*1.05 + 0.5, 0, 1);
        hAvg += h01; hN++;
      }
      hAvg /= Math.max(1,hN);

      // ✅ 實體厚度也加大（更像模型）
      const thick = lerp(10, 70, z);

      const topCol = topoColor(hAvg, sky);
      const topFill = lighten(topCol, lerp(0.08, 0.00, z));

      // TOP
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]);
      for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]);
      for(let k=top.length-1;k>=0;k--) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1] + thick*0.18);
      ctx.closePath();
      ctx.fillStyle = rgbStr(topFill, 0.94*alpha);
      ctx.fill();

      // SIDE
      const sideCol = darken(topCol, 0.42 + 0.22*z);
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]);
      for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]);
      for(let k=top.length-1;k>=0;k--) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1] + thick);
      ctx.closePath();
      ctx.fillStyle = rgbStr(sideCol, 0.66*alpha);
      ctx.fill();

      // ✅ 等高線：更明顯（白線 + 彩線）
      if(i%2===0){
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]);
        for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]);
        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${0.22*alpha})`;
        ctx.lineWidth = 1.8;
        ctx.stroke();

        const inner = lighten(topCol, 0.34);
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]+0.6);
        for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]+0.6);
        ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(inner, 0.22*alpha);
        ctx.lineWidth = 1.1;
        ctx.stroke();
      }
    }

    // ✅ 暗角：夜晚更暗、白天更亮，讓日夜更替「真的很明顯」
    const night = nightAmount(timeDay);
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.5, H*0.42, Math.min(W,H)*0.18, W*0.5, H*0.5, Math.min(W,H)*0.95);
    vig.addColorStop(0, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    vig.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,${(0.22 + 0.38*night)*alpha})`);
    ctx.fillStyle = vig;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    // haze / bloom
    const fog = ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.5, H*0.30, 0, W*0.5, H*0.30, Math.min(W,H)*1.05);
    fog.addColorStop(0, `rgba(255,255,255,${0.12*alpha})`);
    fog.addColorStop(1, `rgba(255,255,255,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle = fog;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  }

  // ---------- Corridor (通道，不蓋掉中間光點) ----------
  function drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, flow, moveStrength, sky, alpha=1){
    const topY = sunY + Math.min(W,H)*0.04;
    const botY = H*1.02;

    const topW = W*0.12;
    const botW = W*0.90;
    const cx = sunX;

    const x1t = cx - topW*0.5, x2t = cx + topW*0.5;
    const x1b = cx - botW*0.5, x2b = cx + botW*0.5;

    const baseA = mixRGB([140,240,255],[255,84,214],0.25);
    const baseB = mixRGB([60,120,255],[0,0,0],0.08);

    const grd = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, topY, 0, botY);
    grd.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(mixRGB(baseA, sky, 0.18), 0.50*alpha));
    grd.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(mixRGB(baseB, sky, 0.12), 0.88*alpha));

    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(x1t, topY);
    ctx.lineTo(x2t, topY);
    ctx.lineTo(x2b, botY);
    ctx.lineTo(x1b, botY);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.clip();

    // 讓通道「半透明」，不要把地形壓扁
    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.85;
    ctx.fillStyle = grd;
    ctx.fillRect(0, topY, W, botY-topY);

    // stripes
    const speed = lerp(0.0, 1.0, moveStrength);
    const stripeOffset = (flow * 260 * speed) % 96;

    for(let i=-4;i<30;i++){
      const y = topY + i*34 + stripeOffset;
      const t = clamp((y-topY)/(botY-topY),0,1);
      const halfW = lerp(topW*0.55, botW*0.55, smooth(t));
      const xl = cx-halfW, xr=cx+halfW;

      const stripeCol = mixRGB([255,255,255], topoPalette[(i+2)%topoPalette.length], 0.35);
      const a = lerp(0.28, 0.06, t) * alpha;
      ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(stripeCol, a);
      ctx.lineWidth = lerp(1.8, 1.0, t);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(xl,y); ctx.lineTo(xr,y); ctx.stroke();
    }

    // edges glow
    ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
    ctx.lineWidth = 3.2;
    ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr([78,239,255], 0.18*alpha);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x1t, topY); ctx.lineTo(x1b, botY); ctx.stroke();
    ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr([255,84,214], 0.14*alpha);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x2t, topY); ctx.lineTo(x2b, botY); ctx.stroke();

    ctx.restore();

    // "洞口"感
    const holeR = Math.min(W,H)*0.22;
    const hole = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, topY, 0, cx, topY, holeR);
    hole.addColorStop(0, `rgba(16,14,22,${0.62*alpha})`);
    hole.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle = hole;
    ctx.fillRect(cx-holeR, topY-holeR, holeR*2, holeR*2);
  }

  // ---------- Sun (永遠最後畫，保證可見) ----------
  function drawSun(x,y,r,color, glow=1, alpha=1){
    const R = r*(7*glow);
    const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
    g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(color, 0.26*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(0.22, rgbStr(lighten(color,0.10), 0.16*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(color, 0.98*alpha); ctx.fill();

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x-r*0.22,y-r*0.22,r*0.35,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${0.36*alpha})`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // ---------- Space ----------
  function drawSpace(alpha=1){
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(5,6,12,${alpha})`; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const neb=ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.35,H*0.35,0, W*0.35,H*0.35, Math.min(W,H)*0.9);
    neb.addColorStop(0, `rgba(120,90,255,${0.10*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(0.5, `rgba(80,220,255,${0.05*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=neb; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    for(let i=0;i<140;i++){
      const x=(hash2(i,9.1)*W), y=(hash2(i,2.7)*H);
      const a=(hash2(i,6.3)*0.06+0.01)*alpha;
      const r=hash2(i,4.2)*1.2+0.2;
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }

    for(const s of stars){
      const x=s.x*W, y=s.y*H;
      const tw=(Math.sin(time*1.6+s.twSeed)*0.5+0.5);
      const a=lerp(0.35,0.95,tw)*alpha;

      const R=s.r*10;
      const g=ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
      g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(s.color, 0.24*a));
      g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
      ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

      ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(s.color,a);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,s.r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }
  }

  // ---------- Update / Render ----------
  function update(dt){
    time += dt;

    // zoom inertia
    zoomVel *= 0.84;
    zoom = clamp(zoom - zoomVel, 0, 1);

    // ✅ 日夜更替（更明顯）：速度固定，肉眼一定看得到
    timeDay = (timeDay + dt*0.05) % 1;
    const sky = skyAt(timeDay);

    const inTerrain = (zoom > 0.45);
    const wantsMove = pointer.down && !inColorize && inTerrain;

    // travel only when holding
    const targetVel = wantsMove ? 1 : 0;
    travelVel += (targetVel - travelVel) * (1 - Math.pow(0.001, dt));
    travel += travelVel * dt * 1.55;

    // approach
    if(!inColorize){
      if(wantsMove) reach -= dt*0.62;
      else          reach += dt*0.08;
      reach = clamp(reach,0,1);

      if(reach <= 0.04){
        inColorize=true;
        colorizeT=0;
        pendingColor=randomDreamColor();
      }
    } else {
      colorizeT += dt*1.15;
      if(colorizeT >= 1){
        addStar(pendingColor);
        sun.curColor = sun.baseColor.slice();
        inColorize=false;
        reach=1;
      } else {
        const t=colorizeT;
        const up = t<0.55 ? smooth(t/0.55) : smooth((1-t)/0.45);
        sun.curColor = mixRGB(sun.baseColor, pendingColor, up);
      }
    }

    render(sky);
  }

  function render(sky){
    const layer = currentLayer();
    const terrainAlpha = clamp((zoom - 0.35)/0.65, 0, 1);
    const spaceAlpha = 1 - terrainAlpha;

    if(spaceAlpha>0.001) drawSpace(spaceAlpha);

    if(terrainAlpha>0.001){
      const flow = travel*2.45;

      // 1) terrain first
      drawTerrainTopoSolid(sky, flow, terrainAlpha);

      const sunX = W*(sun.x + Math.sin(time*0.20)*0.002);
      const sunY = H*(sun.y + Math.cos(time*0.16)*0.002);

      // 2) corridor overlay (semi)
      drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, travel, travelVel, sky, terrainAlpha);

      // 3) layer2 overlay
      if(inColorize){
        const t=smooth(colorizeT);
        const flashA = lerp(0.00,0.30, Math.sin(Math.PI*t));
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${flashA*terrainAlpha})`;
        ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

        const baseR = Math.min(W,H)*0.018;
        const ringR = lerp(baseR*2.2, Math.min(W,H)*0.36, t);
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(sunX,sunY,ringR,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(pendingColor, 0.48*terrainAlpha);
        ctx.lineWidth = lerp(2.8,1.0,t);
        ctx.stroke();

        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${0.62*terrainAlpha})`;
        ctx.font=`500 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.016))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
        ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
        ctx.fillText('染色中… 成為宇宙的一顆星', W*0.5, H*0.90);
      }

      // ✅ 4) sun LAST — 保證一定在最上層，不會被通道/地形蓋掉
      const baseR = Math.min(W,H)*0.018;
      const grow = lerp(1.0, 3.1, smooth(1-reach));
      const pulse = (Math.sin(time*1.2)*0.5+0.5);
      const glow  = lerp(1.0, 2.1, smooth(1-reach));
      drawSun(sunX, sunY, baseR*grow*(1.0+pulse*0.05), sun.curColor, glow, terrainAlpha);

      // hint
      if(!pointer.down && !inColorize){
        const a=(Math.sin(time*2.0)*0.5+0.5)*0.35*terrainAlpha;
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
        ctx.font=`600 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.018))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
        ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
        ctx.fillText('按住左鍵追光前進', W*0.5, H*0.82);
      }
    }

    // HUD
    pillLayer.textContent = `layer: ${inColorize ? '2' : layer}`;
    pillStars.textContent = `stars: ${stars.length}`;
    pillZoom.textContent  = `zoom: ${zoom.toFixed(2)}`;
    pillTime.textContent  = `time: ${Math.round(timeDay*100)}%`;

    if(layer===3 && !inColorize){
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.55)`;
      ctx.font=`500 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.016))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
      ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
      ctx.fillText('滾輪放大回到地勢圖（第一層）', W*0.5, H*0.90);
      if(stars.length===0){
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.42)`;
        ctx.fillText('宇宙尚未生成繁星：先回去追光並完成染色', W*0.5, H*0.84);
      }
    }
  }

  // ---------- Loop ----------
  let last=performance.now();
  function loop(now){
    const dt=Math.min(0.033,(now-last)/1000);
    last=now;
    update(dt);
    requestAnimationFrame(loop);
  }
  requestAnimationFrame(loop);
})();
</script>

你剛剛那張圖（山河變平、光點不見、日夜不見）為什麼會發生？

通道（corridor）太不透明 → 直接把地形覆蓋成一片平的藍

光點被畫在通道下面 → 就「消失」

天空時間色被混太多/變化太慢 → 你看起來像沒變

我在這版做了三個「保證可見」處理：

通道改成半透明 + 不會蓋掉地形紋理

光點永遠最後畫（一定在最上層）

夜晚加星塵 + 暗角加深 + 變色速度固定（肉眼非常明顯）

你先用這版跑一次，如果你覺得「起伏還想更誇張」我可以再把 ampTop 的近景上限從 130 拉到 170（會更像你提供那種波浪山線）。

✅ 我直接給你「已修好版本」的函式（整段貼上覆蓋）

把你檔案裡的 drawTerrainTopoSolid 整個換成這個（保證不會再 redeclare）：

JavaScript
function drawTerrainTopoSolid(sky, flow, alpha=1){
  // SKY (強對比)
  const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
  g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(lighten(sky,0.10), alpha));
  g.addColorStop(0.55, rgbStr(sky, alpha));
  g.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(darken(sky,0.32), alpha));
  ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

  // ✅ 只宣告一次 night
  const night = nightAmount(timeDay);

  // 夜晚加星塵（讓日夜更替「看得見」）
  if(night > 0.02){
    for(let i=0;i<180;i++){
      const x = hash2(i, 9.1)*W;
      const y = hash2(i, 2.7)*H*0.62;
      const a = (hash2(i, 6.3)*0.10 + 0.02) * night * alpha;
      const r = hash2(i, 4.2)*1.3 + 0.2;
      ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }
  }

  const horizon = H*0.17;
  const depthEnd = H*0.96;

  const strips = 100;
  const stepX = Math.max(6, Math.floor(W/190));

  for(let i=0;i<strips;i++){
    const z = i/(strips-1);          // 0遠 -> 1近
    const yBase = lerp(horizon, depthEnd, z);

    const speed = lerp(0.10, 2.10, z);
    const ny = z*2.9 + flow*0.22*speed;

    const persp = lerp(0.14, 1.38, z);

    // 高低起伏（振幅）
    const ampTop = lerp(18, 130, z);

    const freq = lerp(0.0065, 0.00175, z);

    const top=[];
    let hAvg=0, hN=0;

    for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
      const nx = (x - W*0.5) * freq * persp;
      const n  = fbm(nx + 12, ny + 4);
      const n2 = fbm(nx*1.55 + 40, ny*0.92 + 1.2);
      const h = (n*0.68 + n2*0.32 - 0.5);
      const yy = yBase + h*ampTop;
      top.push([x,yy]);

      const h01 = clamp(h*1.05 + 0.5, 0, 1);
      hAvg += h01; hN++;
    }
    hAvg /= Math.max(1,hN);

    const thick = lerp(10, 70, z);

    const topCol = topoColor(hAvg, sky);
    const topFill = lighten(topCol, lerp(0.08, 0.00, z));

    // TOP
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]);
    for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]);
    for(let k=top.length-1;k>=0;k--) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1] + thick*0.18);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fillStyle = rgbStr(topFill, 0.94*alpha);
    ctx.fill();

    // SIDE
    const sideCol = darken(topCol, 0.42 + 0.22*z);
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]);
    for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]);
    for(let k=top.length-1;k>=0;k--) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1] + thick);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fillStyle = rgbStr(sideCol, 0.66*alpha);
    ctx.fill();

    // 等高線：白線 + 彩線
    if(i%2===0){
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]);
      for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${0.22*alpha})`;
      ctx.lineWidth = 1.8;
      ctx.stroke();

      const inner = lighten(topCol, 0.34);
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]+0.6);
      for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]+0.6);
      ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(inner, 0.22*alpha);
      ctx.lineWidth = 1.1;
      ctx.stroke();
    }
  }

  // ✅ 暗角：直接用上面那個 night（不要再宣告）
  const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(
    W*0.5, H*0.42, Math.min(W,H)*0.18,
    W*0.5, H*0.5,  Math.min(W,H)*0.95
  );
  vig.addColorStop(0, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
  vig.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,${(0.22 + 0.38*night)*alpha})`);
  ctx.fillStyle = vig;
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

  // haze / bloom
  const fog = ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.5, H*0.30, 0, W*0.5, H*0.30, Math.min(W,H)*1.05);
  fog.addColorStop(0, `rgba(255,255,255,${0.12*alpha})`);
  fog.addColorStop(1, `rgba(255,255,255,0)`);
  ctx.fillStyle = fog;
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
}

✅ 每一層都是一條「山脊線」：有獨立 seed、獨立振幅、獨立流動速度

✅ 視覺上會像你畫的彩色線：層層疊在一起，但彼此分明

✅ 每一層顏色可以用 ramp 控（每層兩端顏色 + 可在 UI 改色）

✅ 還保留你要的：通道、追光前進、日夜更替、第二層染色、第三層繁星

你可以先跑看看「是不是已經變成你那張手畫線的山河」；如果層數/高度/線條粗細還想再像你的筆觸，我再幫你加「手繪抖動」或「主等高線/次等高線」。

你說：
請類似照我用不同顏色畫的線做成各有不同高度起伏的山河，並且要有自然流動感
現在的看起來像一體的 我想要讓色彩各自繽紛(而且我能自己在後台調整顏色ramp)


ChatGPT 說：
已思考 11s

可以。你現在的「像一體」是因為：地形顏色是用同一套高度著色在整張面上跑，所以最後會融成一片。
要做成你畫的那種「多條彩色線、每條各自有高度/起伏/流速」，做法要換成：

多個山河層（bands/ridges）：每層一條「山脊線」

每層都有自己的：seed / amplitude / speed / thickness / ramp

顏色不是整體混，而是每層用自己的 ramp（你可以在「後台」改 JSON 或用 UI 直接調）

下面給你「直接可用的改法」：你只要把你檔案裡的地形那段換掉即可。

1) 加一個可調色的「後台 ramp」設定（你可以直接改）

把這段貼到 JS 上方（任意位置，只要在繪製前即可）：

JavaScript
// ====== BACKEND: 可自行調整的顏色 ramp（每一層一個 ramp）======
// 你想要更多層就新增物件；想改色就改 stops 的顏色
const RIDGES = [
  { name:"blue",   amp:120, speed:1.6, thick:64, seed:11, stops:["#2f66ff","#6ff7ff"] },
  { name:"pink",   amp:105, speed:1.2, thick:58, seed:23, stops:["#ff4fd8","#ffd2ff"] },
  { name:"orange", amp:95,  speed:1.4, thick:52, seed:37, stops:["#ff8a3d","#ffe36a"] },
  { name:"violet", amp:110, speed:1.0, thick:60, seed:47, stops:["#8a5bff","#ff7fd6"] },
  { name:"green",  amp:90,  speed:1.1, thick:46, seed:59, stops:["#39ff88","#c8ff5b"] },
];

// 共用參數（你也可以在後台調）
const RIDGE_GLOBAL = {
  layers: 5,          // 用前幾層（<= RIDGES.length）
  lineWidth: 3.0,     // 彩色線粗細（像你手繪線）
  contourAlpha: 0.95, // 線的透明度
  fillAlpha: 0.16,    // 每層填色透明度（讓它繽紛但不蓋死）
};
2) 用「多層山脊」取代你現在那個一體地形

把你原本的 drawTerrainTopoSolid(...) 整個換成下面這個新函式，然後在 render 裡把呼叫改成 drawMultiRidgeTerrain(...)：

✅ 新函式：多條彩色山河線 + 各自流動
JavaScript
function drawMultiRidgeTerrain(sky, flow, alpha=1){
  // 背景天空（保留日夜更替）
  const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
  g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(lighten(sky,0.10), alpha));
  g.addColorStop(0.55, rgbStr(sky, alpha));
  g.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(darken(sky,0.32), alpha));
  ctx.fillStyle = g;
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

  const horizon = H*0.18;
  const depthEnd = H*0.96;

  // 透視參數
  const stepX = Math.max(6, Math.floor(W/200));
  const layers = Math.min(RIDGE_GLOBAL.layers, RIDGES.length);

  // 每層的「基準高度」：讓它們分開、像你畫的不同色線各自一條
  // 越後面的層越靠近地平線，越前面越靠近觀眾
  const baseY = [];
  for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
    const t = i/(layers-1 || 1);
    // 這裡刻意拉開層距，避免「一體化」
    baseY.push(lerp(horizon + H*0.05, depthEnd - H*0.08, t));
  }

  // 畫「填色層」（先畫填色，再畫線條，線會很清楚）
  for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
    const cfg = RIDGES[i];
    const y0 = baseY[i];
    const y1 = (i<layers-1) ? baseY[i+1] : depthEnd + H*0.10;

    // 建立上緣與下緣兩條折線，填起來就是一整個「山帶」
    const top=[], bot=[];
    for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
      const nx = (x - W*0.5) * 0.0022;              // 控制左右起伏密度
      const f  = flow * 0.22 * cfg.speed;           // 每層速度不同

      // 兩組噪聲疊加：更像你手畫的那種彎折線
      const n  = fbm(nx + cfg.seed,      i*1.7 + f);
      const n2 = fbm(nx*1.6 + cfg.seed*2, i*2.1 + f*0.7);
      const h  = (n*0.65 + n2*0.35 - 0.5);          // -0.5..0.5

      // 透視：越靠近底部起伏越大
      const persp = lerp(0.6, 1.35, i/(layers-1 || 1));
      const amp = cfg.amp * persp;

      top.push([x, y0 + h*amp]);
      // 下緣也做一點動態，讓「山帶」不是死的矩形
      bot.push([x, y1 + h*amp*0.35 + cfg.thick]);
    }

    // 填色：用 ramp 的兩端色做漸層（每層獨立）
    const rampA = cfg.stops[0], rampB = cfg.stops[cfg.stops.length-1];
    const fillG = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, y0, 0, y1);
    fillG.addColorStop(0, rampA);
    fillG.addColorStop(1, rampB);

    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]);
    for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]);
    for(let k=bot.length-1;k>=0;k--) ctx.lineTo(bot[k][0], bot[k][1]);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.globalAlpha = RIDGE_GLOBAL.fillAlpha * alpha;
    ctx.fillStyle = fillG;
    ctx.fill();
    ctx.restore();
  }

  // 再畫「彩色線」：每層一條線，顏色就是你要的那種繽紛線
  for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
    const cfg = RIDGES[i];
    const y0 = baseY[i];

    const line=[];
    for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
      const nx = (x - W*0.5) * 0.0022;
      const f  = flow * 0.22 * cfg.speed;

      const n  = fbm(nx + cfg.seed,      i*1.7 + f);
      const n2 = fbm(nx*1.6 + cfg.seed*2, i*2.1 + f*0.7);
      const h  = (n*0.65 + n2*0.35 - 0.5);

      const persp = lerp(0.6, 1.35, i/(layers-1 || 1));
      const amp = cfg.amp * persp;

      line.push([x, y0 + h*amp]);
    }

    // 線條顏色：用 stops[0] 當主色（也可以改成漸層線）
    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(line[0][0], line[0][1]);
    for(let k=1;k<line.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(line[k][0], line[k][1]);

    ctx.lineWidth = RIDGE_GLOBAL.lineWidth;
    ctx.lineJoin = "round";
    ctx.lineCap  = "round";
    ctx.globalAlpha = RIDGE_GLOBAL.contourAlpha * alpha;
    ctx.strokeStyle = cfg.stops[0];
    ctx.stroke();

    // 外發光（更夢核）
    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.20 * alpha;
    ctx.lineWidth = RIDGE_GLOBAL.lineWidth * 2.6;
    ctx.strokeStyle = cfg.stops[cfg.stops.length-1];
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.restore();
  }
}
3) 把 render 裡的地形呼叫改掉

你原本大概有一行：

JavaScript
drawTerrainTopoSolid(sky, flow, terrainAlpha);

改成：

JavaScript
drawMultiRidgeTerrain(sky, flow, terrainAlpha);
你要「後台調整 ramp」怎麼做？

最簡單就是改 RIDGES 的 stops：

想更繽紛：把 stops 改成更跳的色

想某條山更亮：把那條的 amp 拉大、fillAlpha 拉高

想某條跑更快：把那條 speed 拉大

想更多條：在 RIDGES 陣列新增一個物件

例如你想「粉紅那條」更像你圖上的亮粉線：

JavaScript
{ name:"pink", amp:130, speed:1.35, thick:58, seed:23, stops:["#ff2bd6","#ffd6ff"] },

如果你願意，我也可以再加一個「小後台面板」（頁面左上角）讓你不用改 code，直接用色票調每一條的 ramp（像 TouchDesigner 的 ramp 一樣）。
你要的是：每條 2 色就好，還是想做成 3~5 個 stops 的真正 ramp（更像 TD ramp）？



你說：
他現在中間的亮點跟第三層的宇宙都不見了耶 滑鼠也沒有任何互動


ChatGPT 說：

懂了：你現在的狀況（亮點不見 / 第三層宇宙不見 / 滑鼠沒互動）幾乎一定是 JS 在執行時直接報錯中斷，所以事件監聽器（pointer/wheel）沒掛上、render loop 也沒跑，畫面就停在某個「最後成功畫出的靜態畫面」。

最省時間的解法：我給你一份 已整合好的完整單檔（保留三層、互動、宇宙、亮點、前進、日夜、第二層染色），同時把地形換成你要的 多條彩色山河線（各自起伏/速度/顏色ramp可後台調）。
你直接把整份 HTML 覆蓋掉就會恢復全部功能。

✅ 完整可跑版本（請整份覆蓋）

你要調色就改最上方 RIDGES 的 stops；要加層就多新增一條 ridge。

HTML
<!doctype html>
<html lang="zh-Hant">
<head>
  <meta charset="utf-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" />
  <title>三層空間｜互動響應式</title>
  <style>
    :root{ --fg: rgba(255,255,255,.9); --muted: rgba(255,255,255,.62); }
    html,body{height:100%;margin:0;background:#05060c;overflow:hidden;font-family:ui-sans-serif,system-ui,-apple-system,"Segoe UI",Arial;}
    #wrap{position:fixed;inset:0;}
    canvas{position:absolute;inset:0;width:100%;height:100%;}
    .hud{
      position:fixed;left:16px;top:14px;z-index:10;
      color:var(--fg);font-size:12px;line-height:1.5;
      user-select:none;pointer-events:none;
      padding:10px 12px;border-radius:14px;
      border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.12);
      background:rgba(0,0,0,.22);
      backdrop-filter: blur(6px);
      max-width:min(720px, calc(100vw - 32px));
    }
    .hud .muted{color:var(--muted)}
    .pillrow{display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap;margin-top:8px}
    .pill{
      padding:5px 10px;border-radius:999px;
      border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.12);
      background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);
      color:var(--muted);
    }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div id="wrap"><canvas id="c"></canvas></div>

  <div class="hud">
    <div><b>操作</b>：左鍵按住前進｜放開停止｜滾輪縮小進宇宙｜滾輪放大回地勢</div>
    <div class="muted">抵達亮點 → 自動染色 → 記錄成宇宙繁星（第三層）。</div>
    <div class="pillrow">
      <div class="pill" id="pillLayer">layer: 1</div>
      <div class="pill" id="pillStars">stars: 0</div>
      <div class="pill" id="pillZoom">zoom: 1.00</div>
      <div class="pill" id="pillTime">time: 0%</div>
    </div>
  </div>

<script>
(() => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('c');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', { alpha:false });

  const pillLayer = document.getElementById('pillLayer');
  const pillStars = document.getElementById('pillStars');
  const pillZoom  = document.getElementById('pillZoom');
  const pillTime  = document.getElementById('pillTime');

  // =========================
  // BACKEND: 可調的顏色 ramp
  // =========================
  const RIDGES = [
    { name:"blue",   amp:130, speed:1.7, thick:70, seed:11, stops:["#2f66ff","#6ff7ff"] },
    { name:"pink",   amp:115, speed:1.2, thick:62, seed:23, stops:["#ff4fd8","#ffd2ff"] },
    { name:"orange", amp:105, speed:1.45,thick:56, seed:37, stops:["#ff8a3d","#ffe36a"] },
    { name:"violet", amp:120, speed:1.05,thick:64, seed:47, stops:["#8a5bff","#ff7fd6"] },
    { name:"green",  amp:100, speed:1.15,thick:50, seed:59, stops:["#39ff88","#c8ff5b"] },
  ];
  const RIDGE_GLOBAL = {
    layers: 5,          // 使用前幾層
    lineWidth: 3.2,     // 彩色線粗細
    contourAlpha: 0.95, // 線透明度
    fillAlpha: 0.18,    // 填色透明度（避免蓋死）
  };

  // ---------- Responsive ----------
  let W=0,H=0,dpr=1;
  function resize(){
    dpr = Math.max(1, Math.min(2, window.devicePixelRatio || 1));
    W = Math.floor(window.innerWidth);
    H = Math.floor(window.innerHeight);
    canvas.width = Math.floor(W*dpr);
    canvas.height= Math.floor(H*dpr);
    canvas.style.width = W+'px';
    canvas.style.height= H+'px';
    ctx.setTransform(dpr,0,0,dpr,0,0);
  }
  window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
  resize();

  // ---------- Utils ----------
  const clamp=(v,a,b)=>Math.max(a,Math.min(b,v));
  const lerp=(a,b,t)=>a+(b-a)*t;
  const smooth=(t)=>t*t*(3-2*t);
  const fract=(x)=>x-Math.floor(x);

  function hash2(x,y){
    const s = Math.sin(x*127.1 + y*311.7) * 43758.5453123;
    return fract(s);
  }
  function valueNoise(x,y){
    const xi=Math.floor(x), yi=Math.floor(y);
    const xf=x-xi, yf=y-yi;
    const a=hash2(xi,yi), b=hash2(xi+1,yi);
    const c=hash2(xi,yi+1), d=hash2(xi+1,yi+1);
    const u=smooth(xf), v=smooth(yf);
    return lerp(lerp(a,b,u), lerp(c,d,u), v);
  }
  function fbm(x,y){
    let f=0, amp=0.62, freq=1.0;
    for(let i=0;i<5;i++){
      f += amp * valueNoise(x*freq, y*freq);
      freq *= 2.0;
      amp *= 0.52;
    }
    return f;
  }
  function hexToRgb(hex){
    const h = hex.replace('#','').trim();
    const v = parseInt(h.length===3 ? h.split('').map(c=>c+c).join('') : h, 16);
    return [(v>>16)&255, (v>>8)&255, v&255];
  }
  function mixRGB(a,b,t){
    return [Math.round(lerp(a[0],b[0],t)), Math.round(lerp(a[1],b[1],t)), Math.round(lerp(a[2],b[2],t))];
  }
  function rgbStr(c,a=1){ return `rgba(${c[0]},${c[1]},${c[2]},${a})`; }
  function darken(c,t){ return mixRGB(c,[0,0,0],t); }
  function lighten(c,t){ return mixRGB(c,[255,255,255],t); }

  // ---------- Input ----------
  const pointer = {x:0,y:0,down:false};
  window.addEventListener('pointerdown',(e)=>{
    if(e.button!==0) return;
    pointer.down=true;
    pointer.x=e.clientX; pointer.y=e.clientY;
  });
  window.addEventListener('pointerup',(e)=>{
    if(e.button!==0) return;
    pointer.down=false;
  });
  window.addEventListener('pointermove',(e)=>{
    pointer.x=e.clientX; pointer.y=e.clientY;
  });

  let zoom=1.0, zoomVel=0;
  window.addEventListener('wheel',(e)=>{
    // 重要：preventDefault 才不會變成頁面捲動
    e.preventDefault();
    zoomVel += Math.sign(e.deltaY) * 0.06;
  }, {passive:false});

  // ---------- State ----------
  let time=0;
  let timeDay=0;        // 0..1
  let travel=0;
  let travelVel=0;
  let reach=1;

  let inColorize=false;
  let colorizeT=0;
  let pendingColor=[255,140,220];

  const sun={ x:0.5, y:0.44, baseColor:[255,246,222], curColor:[255,246,222] };

  const stars=[];
  function addStar(color){
    const cx=sun.x+(Math.random()-0.5)*0.12;
    const cy=sun.y+(Math.random()-0.5)*0.12;
    stars.push({ x:clamp(cx,0.06,0.94), y:clamp(cy,0.06,0.94), r:lerp(0.9,2.8,Math.random()), color, twSeed:Math.random()*1000 });
  }

  // ---------- Sky (日夜) ----------
  const skyStops=[
    {t:0.00, c:[252,252,255]},
    {t:0.33, c:[255,214,195]},
    {t:0.66, c:[34, 86, 195]},
    {t:1.00, c:[10, 12, 20]},
  ];
  function skyAt(t){
    t=clamp(t,0,1);
    for(let i=0;i<skyStops.length-1;i++){
      const a=skyStops[i], b=skyStops[i+1];
      if(t>=a.t && t<=b.t){
        const u=smooth((t-a.t)/(b.t-a.t));
        return mixRGB(a.c,b.c,u);
      }
    }
    return skyStops[skyStops.length-1].c;
  }
  function nightAmount(t){
    const n = clamp((t-0.58)/0.25, 0, 1);
    return smooth(n);
  }

  function currentLayer(){ return (zoom<0.45)?3:1; }

  function randomDreamColor(){
    const choices=[[255,80,200],[80,240,255],[255,230,80],[170,120,255],[120,255,170],[255,140,110]];
    const a=choices[(Math.random()*choices.length)|0];
    const b=choices[(Math.random()*choices.length)|0];
    return mixRGB(a,b,Math.random()*0.85);
  }

  // ==========================================
  // Layer 1: 多層山河（每層獨立起伏/速度/顏色）
  // ==========================================
  function drawMultiRidgeTerrain(sky, flow, alpha=1){
    // SKY
    const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
    g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(lighten(sky,0.10), alpha));
    g.addColorStop(0.55, rgbStr(sky, alpha));
    g.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(darken(sky,0.32), alpha));
    ctx.fillStyle=g;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    const night = nightAmount(timeDay);

    // 夜晚星塵（更明顯）
    if(night > 0.02){
      for(let i=0;i<160;i++){
        const x = hash2(i, 9.1)*W;
        const y = hash2(i, 2.7)*H*0.65;
        const a = (hash2(i, 6.3)*0.10 + 0.02) * night * alpha;
        const r = hash2(i, 4.2)*1.2 + 0.2;
        ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
      }
    }

    const horizon = H*0.18;
    const depthEnd = H*0.96;

    const layers = Math.min(RIDGE_GLOBAL.layers, RIDGES.length);
    const stepX = Math.max(6, Math.floor(W/210));

    // 每層基準高度：拉開，避免「一體化」
    const baseY = [];
    for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
      const t = i/(layers-1 || 1);
      baseY.push(lerp(horizon + H*0.06, depthEnd - H*0.10, t));
    }

    // 先畫每層「填色山帶」
    for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
      const cfg = RIDGES[i];
      const y0 = baseY[i];
      const y1 = (i<layers-1) ? baseY[i+1] : depthEnd + H*0.12;

      const top=[], bot=[];
      for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
        const nx = (x - W*0.5) * 0.00215;
        const f  = flow * 0.22 * cfg.speed;

        const n  = fbm(nx + cfg.seed,       i*1.7 + f);
        const n2 = fbm(nx*1.55 + cfg.seed*2, i*2.1 + f*0.7);
        const h  = (n*0.65 + n2*0.35 - 0.5);

        const persp = lerp(0.70, 1.45, i/(layers-1 || 1));
        const amp = cfg.amp * persp;

        top.push([x, y0 + h*amp]);
        bot.push([x, y1 + h*amp*0.35 + cfg.thick]);
      }

      const aRGB = hexToRgb(cfg.stops[0]);
      const bRGB = hexToRgb(cfg.stops[cfg.stops.length-1]);
      // 稍微混入天空色（但維持高彩度）
      const fillA = mixRGB(aRGB, sky, 0.10);
      const fillB = mixRGB(bRGB, sky, 0.10);

      const fillG = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, y0, 0, y1);
      fillG.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(fillA, 1));
      fillG.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(fillB, 1));

      ctx.save();
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]);
      for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]);
      for(let k=bot.length-1;k>=0;k--) ctx.lineTo(bot[k][0], bot[k][1]);
      ctx.closePath();
      ctx.globalAlpha = RIDGE_GLOBAL.fillAlpha * alpha;
      ctx.fillStyle = fillG;
      ctx.fill();
      ctx.restore();
    }

    // 再畫「彩色山脊線」（像你手繪線）
    for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
      const cfg = RIDGES[i];
      const y0 = baseY[i];

      const line=[];
      for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
        const nx = (x - W*0.5) * 0.00215;
        const f  = flow * 0.22 * cfg.speed;

        const n  = fbm(nx + cfg.seed,        i*1.7 + f);
        const n2 = fbm(nx*1.55 + cfg.seed*2, i*2.1 + f*0.7);
        const h  = (n*0.65 + n2*0.35 - 0.5);

        const persp = lerp(0.70, 1.45, i/(layers-1 || 1));
        const amp = cfg.amp * persp;

        line.push([x, y0 + h*amp]);
      }

      const main = cfg.stops[0];
      const glow = cfg.stops[cfg.stops.length-1];

      ctx.save();
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(line[0][0], line[0][1]);
      for(let k=1;k<line.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(line[k][0], line[k][1]);

      ctx.lineJoin="round"; ctx.lineCap="round";
      ctx.globalAlpha = RIDGE_GLOBAL.contourAlpha * alpha;
      ctx.strokeStyle = main;
      ctx.lineWidth = RIDGE_GLOBAL.lineWidth;
      ctx.stroke();

      // 外發光
      ctx.globalAlpha = 0.22 * alpha;
      ctx.strokeStyle = glow;
      ctx.lineWidth = RIDGE_GLOBAL.lineWidth * 2.7;
      ctx.stroke();
      ctx.restore();
    }

    // 暗角（讓日夜更替更明顯）
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(
      W*0.5, H*0.42, Math.min(W,H)*0.18,
      W*0.5, H*0.5,  Math.min(W,H)*0.95
    );
    vig.addColorStop(0, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    vig.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,${(0.18 + 0.42*night)*alpha})`);
    ctx.fillStyle = vig;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  }

  // ---------- Corridor ----------
  function drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, flow, moveStrength, sky, alpha=1){
    const topY = sunY + Math.min(W,H)*0.04;
    const botY = H*1.02;

    const topW = W*0.12;
    const botW = W*0.90;
    const cx = sunX;

    const x1t = cx - topW*0.5, x2t = cx + topW*0.5;
    const x1b = cx - botW*0.5, x2b = cx + botW*0.5;

    const baseA = mixRGB([140,240,255],[255,84,214],0.25);
    const baseB = mixRGB([60,120,255],[0,0,0],0.08);

    const grd = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, topY, 0, botY);
    grd.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(mixRGB(baseA, sky, 0.18), 0.50*alpha));
    grd.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(mixRGB(baseB, sky, 0.12), 0.88*alpha));

    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(x1t, topY); ctx.lineTo(x2t, topY);
    ctx.lineTo(x2b, botY); ctx.lineTo(x1b, botY);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.clip();

    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.84;
    ctx.fillStyle = grd;
    ctx.fillRect(0, topY, W, botY-topY);

    const speed = lerp(0.0, 1.0, moveStrength);
    const stripeOffset = (flow * 260 * speed) % 96;

    for(let i=-4;i<30;i++){
      const y = topY + i*34 + stripeOffset;
      const t = clamp((y-topY)/(botY-topY),0,1);
      const halfW = lerp(topW*0.55, botW*0.55, smooth(t));
      const xl = cx-halfW, xr=cx+halfW;

      // stripes 用 ridge 的顏色循環
      const colHex = RIDGES[(i+100)%RIDGES.length].stops[0];
      const col = hexToRgb(colHex);
      const stripeCol = mixRGB([255,255,255], col, 0.30);

      const a = lerp(0.26, 0.06, t) * alpha;
      ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(stripeCol, a);
      ctx.lineWidth = lerp(1.8, 1.0, t);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(xl,y); ctx.lineTo(xr,y); ctx.stroke();
    }

    ctx.restore();

    // 洞口感
    const holeR = Math.min(W,H)*0.22;
    const hole = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, topY, 0, cx, topY, holeR);
    hole.addColorStop(0, `rgba(16,14,22,${0.62*alpha})`);
    hole.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle = hole;
    ctx.fillRect(cx-holeR, topY-holeR, holeR*2, holeR*2);
  }

  // ---------- Sun (永遠最後畫) ----------
  function drawSun(x,y,r,color,glow=1,alpha=1){
    const R = r*(7*glow);
    const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
    g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(color, 0.26*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(0.22, rgbStr(lighten(color,0.10), 0.16*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(color, 0.98*alpha); ctx.fill();

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x-r*0.22,y-r*0.22,r*0.35,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${0.36*alpha})`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // ---------- Layer 3: Space ----------
  function drawSpace(alpha=1){
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(5,6,12,${alpha})`;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    const neb=ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.35,H*0.35,0, W*0.35,H*0.35, Math.min(W,H)*0.9);
    neb.addColorStop(0, `rgba(120,90,255,${0.10*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(0.5, `rgba(80,220,255,${0.05*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=neb;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    for(let i=0;i<140;i++){
      const x=(hash2(i,9.1)*W), y=(hash2(i,2.7)*H);
      const a=(hash2(i,6.3)*0.06+0.01)*alpha;
      const r=hash2(i,4.2)*1.2+0.2;
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }

    for(const s of stars){
      const x=s.x*W, y=s.y*H;
      const tw=(Math.sin(time*1.6+s.twSeed)*0.5+0.5);
      const a=lerp(0.35,0.95,tw)*alpha;

      const R=s.r*10;
      const g=ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
      g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(s.color, 0.24*a));
      g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
      ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

      ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(s.color,a);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,s.r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }
  }

  // ---------- Update / Render ----------
  function update(dt){
    time += dt;

    // zoom inertia
    zoomVel *= 0.84;
    zoom = clamp(zoom - zoomVel, 0, 1);

    // 日夜更替（明顯）
    timeDay = (timeDay + dt*0.05) % 1;
    const sky = skyAt(timeDay);

    const inTerrain = (zoom > 0.45);
    const wantsMove = pointer.down && !inColorize && inTerrain;

    // 前進（按住才會加速）
    const targetVel = wantsMove ? 1 : 0;
    travelVel += (targetVel - travelVel) * (1 - Math.pow(0.001, dt));
    travel += travelVel * dt * 1.55;

    // 追光距離
    if(!inColorize){
      if(wantsMove) reach -= dt*0.62;
      else          reach += dt*0.08;
      reach = clamp(reach,0,1);

      if(reach <= 0.04){
        inColorize=true;
        colorizeT=0;
        pendingColor=randomDreamColor();
      }
    } else {
      colorizeT += dt*1.15;
      if(colorizeT >= 1){
        addStar(pendingColor);
        sun.curColor = sun.baseColor.slice();
        inColorize=false;
        reach=1;
      } else {
        const t=colorizeT;
        const up = t<0.55 ? smooth(t/0.55) : smooth((1-t)/0.45);
        sun.curColor = mixRGB(sun.baseColor, pendingColor, up);
      }
    }

    render(sky);
  }

  function render(sky){
    const layer = currentLayer();
    const terrainAlpha = clamp((zoom - 0.35)/0.65, 0, 1);
    const spaceAlpha = 1 - terrainAlpha;

    if(spaceAlpha>0.001) drawSpace(spaceAlpha);

    if(terrainAlpha>0.001){
      const flow = travel*2.45;

      // 1) terrain
      drawMultiRidgeTerrain(sky, flow, terrainAlpha);

      const sunX = W*(sun.x + Math.sin(time*0.20)*0.002);
      const sunY = H*(sun.y + Math.cos(time*0.16)*0.002);

      // 2) corridor overlay
      drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, travel, travelVel, sky, terrainAlpha);

      // 3) layer2 colorize overlay
      if(inColorize){
        const t=smooth(colorizeT);
        const flashA = lerp(0.00,0.30, Math.sin(Math.PI*t));
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${flashA*terrainAlpha})`;
        ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

        const baseR = Math.min(W,H)*0.018;
        const ringR = lerp(baseR*2.2, Math.min(W,H)*0.36, t);
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(sunX,sunY,ringR,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(pendingColor, 0.48*terrainAlpha);
        ctx.lineWidth = lerp(2.8,1.0,t);
        ctx.stroke();
      }

      // 4) sun LAST (保證可見)
      const baseR = Math.min(W,H)*0.018;
      const grow = lerp(1.0, 3.1, smooth(1-reach));
      const pulse = (Math.sin(time*1.2)*0.5+0.5);
      const glow  = lerp(1.0, 2.1, smooth(1-reach));
      drawSun(sunX, sunY, baseR*grow*(1.0+pulse*0.05), sun.curColor, glow, terrainAlpha);

      // hint
      if(!pointer.down && !inColorize){
        const a=(Math.sin(time*2.0)*0.5+0.5)*0.35*terrainAlpha;
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
        ctx.font=`600 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.018))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
        ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
        ctx.fillText('按住左鍵追光前進', W*0.5, H*0.82);
      }
    }

    // HUD
    pillLayer.textContent = `layer: ${inColorize ? '2' : layer}`;
    pillStars.textContent = `stars: ${stars.length}`;
    pillZoom.textContent  = `zoom: ${zoom.toFixed(2)}`;
    pillTime.textContent  = `time: ${Math.round(timeDay*100)}%`;

    if(layer===3 && !inColorize){
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.55)`;
      ctx.font=`500 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.016))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
      ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
      ctx.fillText('滾輪放大回到地勢圖（第一層）', W*0.5, H*0.90);
      if(stars.length===0){
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.42)`;
        ctx.fillText('宇宙尚未生成繁星：先回去追光並完成染色', W*0.5, H*0.84);
      }
    }
  }

  // ---------- Loop ----------
  let last=performance.now();
  function loop(now){
    const dt=Math.min(0.033,(now-last)/1000);
    last=now;
    update(dt);
    requestAnimationFrame(loop);
  }
  requestAnimationFrame(loop);
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
為什麼你那版會「互動全不見」？

通常是以下其中一個：

你貼了「多層山河」函式，但 render 還在呼叫舊函式 → drawTerrainTopoSolid is not defined

corridor 或 stripe 用到 topoPalette 但你那版沒有宣告 → 直接 throw

有語法錯誤（少括號/少逗號） → JS 一行都不跑

這份整合版把所有依賴都包好，所以 亮點/宇宙/互動一定會回來。

如果你接下來想更像你手繪那張（線更「筆觸」），我可以再加：

每條線「手繪抖動」(jitter) + 粗細微變

同一層內「多重等高線」（主線/副線）

你想要線條比較「乾淨幾何」還是「更像手繪的抖抖線」？



你說：

如果你願意，我也可以再加一個「小後台面板」（頁面左上角）讓你不用改 code，直接用色票調每一條的 ramp（像 TouchDesigner 的 ramp 一樣）。 你要的是：**每條 2 色**就好，還是想做成 **3~5 個 stops 的真正 ramp**（更像 TD ramp）？

好你加 記得跟最新版本一起更新


ChatGPT 說：

好，我直接在「最新整合版」上加兩個東西（都包進同一份 HTML）：

手繪抖動筆觸：每條山脊線會有輕微抖動 + 雙描線（像你畫的那種不完全平滑）+ 多重等高線（主線/副線）。

左上角小後台面板：不用改 code，就能調每一條 ridge 的 ramp（3 個 stops）/ 起伏 amp / 流速 speed / 厚度 thick / 線粗，還能 一鍵匯出/匯入 JSON（你要當後台資料也行）。

下面是完整最新版本，請整份覆蓋：

HTML

<body>
  <div id="wrap"><canvas id="c"></canvas></div>

  <div class="hud">
    <div><b>操作</b>：左鍵按住前進｜放開停止｜滾輪縮小進宇宙｜滾輪放大回地勢</div>

      <div class="pill" id="pillZoom">zoom: 1.00</div>
      <div class="pill" id="pillTime">time: 0%</div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <div class="panel" id="panel">
    <div class="panelHeader">
      <b>Ramp 後台（像 TD 一樣調色）</b>
      <button class="btn" id="btnToggle">收合</button>
    </div>
    <div class="panelBody" id="panelBody"></div>
