<script>
(() => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('c');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', { alpha:false });

  const pillLayer = document.getElementById('pillLayer');
  const pillStars = document.getElementById('pillStars');
  const pillZoom  = document.getElementById('pillZoom');
  const pillTime  = document.getElementById('pillTime');

  // =========================
  // BACKEND: 可調的顏色 ramp（每層 3 stops）
  // =========================
  const STATE = {
    ridges: [
      { name:"blue",   amp:130, speed:1.7, thick:70, seed:11, stops:["#2f66ff","#6ff7ff","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"pink",   amp:115, speed:1.2, thick:62, seed:23, stops:["#ff4fd8","#ffd2ff","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"orange", amp:105, speed:1.45,thick:56, seed:37, stops:["#ff8a3d","#ffe36a","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"violet", amp:120, speed:1.05,thick:64, seed:47, stops:["#8a5bff","#ff7fd6","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"green",  amp:100, speed:1.15,thick:50, seed:59, stops:["#39ff88","#c8ff5b","#ffffff"] },
    ],
    global: {
      layers: 5,
      lineWidth: 3.2,
      contourAlpha: 0.95,
      fillAlpha: 0.18,

      // 手繪筆觸參數
      handJitter: 2.2,      // 抖動強度(px)
      handWobble: 0.9,      // 流動擺動強度
      multiContours: 3,     // 幾條副等高線（含主線）
      contourSpacing: 2.2,  // 副線間距(px)
      sketchDouble: true,   // 雙描線（更像手繪）
    }
  };

  // ---------- Responsive ----------
  let W=0,H=0,dpr=1;
  function resize(){
    dpr = Math.max(1, Math.min(2, window.devicePixelRatio || 1));
    W = Math.floor(window.innerWidth);
    H = Math.floor(window.innerHeight);
    canvas.width = Math.floor(W*dpr);
    canvas.height= Math.floor(H*dpr);
    canvas.style.width = W+'px';
    canvas.style.height= H+'px';
    ctx.setTransform(dpr,0,0,dpr,0,0);
  }
  window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
  resize();

  // ---------- Utils ----------
  const clamp=(v,a,b)=>Math.max(a,Math.min(b,v));
  const lerp=(a,b,t)=>a+(b-a)*t;
  const smooth=(t)=>t*t*(3-2*t);
  const fract=(x)=>x-Math.floor(x);

  function hash2(x,y){
    const s = Math.sin(x*127.1 + y*311.7) * 43758.5453123;
    return fract(s);
  }
  function valueNoise(x,y){
    const xi=Math.floor(x), yi=Math.floor(y);
    const xf=x-xi, yf=y-yi;
    const a=hash2(xi,yi), b=hash2(xi+1,yi);
    const c=hash2(xi,yi+1), d=hash2(xi+1,yi+1);
    const u=smooth(xf), v=smooth(yf);
    return lerp(lerp(a,b,u), lerp(c,d,u), v);
  }
  function fbm(x,y){
    let f=0, amp=0.62, freq=1.0;
    for(let i=0;i<5;i++){
      f += amp * valueNoise(x*freq, y*freq);
      freq *= 2.0;
      amp *= 0.52;
    }
    return f;
  }
  function hexToRgb(hex){
    const h = hex.replace('#','').trim();
    const v = parseInt(h.length===3 ? h.split('').map(c=>c+c).join('') : h, 16);
    return [(v>>16)&255, (v>>8)&255, v&255];
  }
  function mixRGB(a,b,t){
    return [Math.round(lerp(a[0],b[0],t)), Math.round(lerp(a[1],b[1],t)), Math.round(lerp(a[2],b[2],t))];
  }
  function rgbStr(c,a=1){ return `rgba(${c[0]},${c[1]},${c[2]},${a})`; }
  function darken(c,t){ return mixRGB(c,[0,0,0],t); }
  function lighten(c,t){ return mixRGB(c,[255,255,255],t); }

  // ---------- Input ----------
  const pointer = {x:0,y:0,down:false};
  window.addEventListener('pointerdown',(e)=>{
    if(e.button!==0) return;
    pointer.down=true;
    pointer.x=e.clientX; pointer.y=e.clientY;
  });
  window.addEventListener('pointerup',(e)=>{
    if(e.button!==0) return;
    pointer.down=false;
  });
  window.addEventListener('pointermove',(e)=>{
    pointer.x=e.clientX; pointer.y=e.clientY;
  });

  let zoom=1.0, zoomVel=0;
  window.addEventListener('wheel',(e)=>{
    e.preventDefault();
    zoomVel += Math.sign(e.deltaY) * 0.06;
  }, {passive:false});

  // ---------- State ----------
  let time=0;
  let timeDay=0;        // 0..1
  let travel=0;
  let travelVel=0;
  let reach=1;

  let inColorize=false;
  let colorizeT=0;
  let pendingColor=[255,140,220];

  const sun={ x:0.5, y:0.44, baseColor:[255,246,222], curColor:[255,246,222] };

  const stars=[];
  function addStar(color){
    const cx=sun.x+(Math.random()-0.5)*0.12;
    const cy=sun.y+(Math.random()-0.5)*0.12;
    stars.push({ x:clamp(cx,0.06,0.94), y:clamp(cy,0.06,0.94), r:lerp(0.9,2.8,Math.random()), color, twSeed:Math.random()*1000 });
  }

  // ---------- Sky (日夜) ----------
  const skyStops=[
    {t:0.00, c:[252,252,255]},
    {t:0.33, c:[255,214,195]},
    {t:0.66, c:[34, 86, 195]},
    {t:1.00, c:[10, 12, 20]},
  ];
  function skyAt(t){
    t=clamp(t,0,1);
    for(let i=0;i<skyStops.length-1;i++){
      const a=skyStops[i], b=skyStops[i+1];
      if(t>=a.t && t<=b.t){
        const u=smooth((t-a.t)/(b.t-a.t));
        return mixRGB(a.c,b.c,u);
      }
    }
    return skyStops[skyStops.length-1].c;
  }
  function nightAmount(t){
    const n = clamp((t-0.58)/0.25, 0, 1);
    return smooth(n);
  }

  function currentLayer(){ return (zoom<0.45)?3:1; }

  function randomDreamColor(){
    const choices=[[255,80,200],[80,240,255],[255,230,80],[170,120,255],[120,255,170],[255,140,110]];
    const a=choices[(Math.random()*choices.length)|0];
    const b=choices[(Math.random()*choices.length)|0];
    return mixRGB(a,b,Math.random()*0.85);
  }

  // ==========================================
  // Layer 1: 多層山河（每層獨立）＋手繪筆觸
  // ==========================================
  function drawMultiRidgeTerrain(sky, flow, alpha=1){
    // SKY
    const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
    g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(lighten(sky,0.10), alpha));
    g.addColorStop(0.55, rgbStr(sky, alpha));
    g.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(darken(sky,0.32), alpha));
    ctx.fillStyle=g;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    const night = nightAmount(timeDay);

    // 夜晚星塵（更明顯）
    if(night > 0.02){
      for(let i=0;i<160;i++){
        const x = hash2(i, 9.1)*W;
        const y = hash2(i, 2.7)*H*0.65;
        const a = (hash2(i, 6.3)*0.10 + 0.02) * night * alpha;
        const r = hash2(i, 4.2)*1.2 + 0.2;
        ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
      }
    }

    const horizon = H*0.18;
    const depthEnd = H*0.96;

    const G = STATE.global;
    const ridges = STATE.ridges;
    const layers = Math.min(G.layers, ridges.length);
    const stepX = Math.max(6, Math.floor(W/210));

    // 每層基準高度：拉開，避免一體化
    const baseY = [];
    for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
      const t = i/(layers-1 || 1);
      baseY.push(lerp(horizon + H*0.06, depthEnd - H*0.10, t));
    }

    // ---- fill bands ----
    for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
      const cfg = ridges[i];
      const y0 = baseY[i];
      const y1 = (i<layers-1) ? baseY[i+1] : depthEnd + H*0.12;

      const top=[], bot=[];
      for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
        const nx = (x - W*0.5) * 0.00215;
        const f  = flow * 0.22 * cfg.speed;

        const n  = fbm(nx + cfg.seed,        i*1.7 + f);
        const n2 = fbm(nx*1.55 + cfg.seed*2, i*2.1 + f*0.7);
        const h  = (n*0.65 + n2*0.35 - 0.5);

        const persp = lerp(0.70, 1.45, i/(layers-1 || 1));
        const amp = cfg.amp * persp;

        // 手繪微抖（但不要把形狀弄壞）
        const jitter = (hash2(x*0.05, i*33.3) - 0.5) * G.handJitter;
        const wob = Math.sin((x*0.012) + time*0.6 + i*1.3) * G.handWobble;

        top.push([x, y0 + h*amp + jitter + wob]);
        bot.push([x, y1 + h*amp*0.35 + cfg.thick + jitter*0.35]);
      }

      // ramp: 3 stops
      const c0 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[0]), sky, 0.10);
      const c1 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[1]), sky, 0.10);
      const c2 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[2]), sky, 0.10);

      const fillG = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, y0, 0, y1);
      fillG.addColorStop(0,   rgbStr(c0,1));
      fillG.addColorStop(0.5, rgbStr(c1,1));
      fillG.addColorStop(1,   rgbStr(c2,1));

      ctx.save();
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]);
      for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]);
      for(let k=bot.length-1;k>=0;k--) ctx.lineTo(bot[k][0], bot[k][1]);
      ctx.closePath();
      ctx.globalAlpha = G.fillAlpha * alpha;
      ctx.fillStyle = fillG;
      ctx.fill();
      ctx.restore();
    }

    // ---- contour lines (multi) ----
    for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
      const cfg = ridges[i];
      const y0 = baseY[i];

      // 先算出主線點
      const line=[];
      for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
        const nx = (x - W*0.5) * 0.00215;
        const f  = flow * 0.22 * cfg.speed;

        const n  = fbm(nx + cfg.seed,        i*1.7 + f);
        const n2 = fbm(nx*1.55 + cfg.seed*2, i*2.1 + f*0.7);
        const h  = (n*0.65 + n2*0.35 - 0.5);

        const persp = lerp(0.70, 1.45, i/(layers-1 || 1));
        const amp = cfg.amp * persp;

        const jitter = (hash2(x*0.05, i*33.3+9.9) - 0.5) * G.handJitter;
        const wob = Math.sin((x*0.012) + time*0.6 + i*1.3) * G.handWobble;

        line.push([x, y0 + h*amp + jitter + wob]);
      }

      // 線用「沿線漸層」更繽紛
      const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, y0, W, y0);
      grad.addColorStop(0,   cfg.stops[0]);
      grad.addColorStop(0.5, cfg.stops[1]);
      grad.addColorStop(1,   cfg.stops[2]);

      const mainAlpha = G.contourAlpha * alpha;
      const count = Math.max(1, Math.floor(G.multiContours));
      const spacing = G.contourSpacing;

      // 畫多條等高線（主線+副線）
      for(let ci=0; ci<count; ci++){
        const off = (ci - (count-1)/2) * spacing;

        ctx.save();
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(line[0][0], line[0][1] + off);
        for(let k=1;k<line.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(line[k][0], line[k][1] + off);

        ctx.lineJoin="round"; ctx.lineCap="round";
        ctx.globalAlpha = (ci===Math.floor((count-1)/2) ? mainAlpha : mainAlpha*0.35);
        ctx.strokeStyle = grad;
        ctx.lineWidth = (ci===Math.floor((count-1)/2) ? G.lineWidth : Math.max(1.1, G.lineWidth*0.62));
        ctx.stroke();

        // 外發光
        ctx.globalAlpha = (ci===Math.floor((count-1)/2) ? 0.18 : 0.10) * alpha;
        ctx.strokeStyle = cfg.stops[1];
        ctx.lineWidth = (ci===Math.floor((count-1)/2) ? G.lineWidth*2.7 : G.lineWidth*2.0);
        ctx.stroke();

        // 手繪雙描線（微偏移再描一次）
        if(G.sketchDouble && ci===Math.floor((count-1)/2)){
          const dx = (hash2(i*9.7, 1.3)-0.5)*1.4;
          const dy = (hash2(i*9.7, 8.1)-0.5)*1.4;
          ctx.globalAlpha = 0.22 * alpha;
          ctx.strokeStyle = cfg.stops[0];
          ctx.lineWidth = Math.max(1.2, G.lineWidth*0.95);
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(line[0][0]+dx, line[0][1]+dy);
          for(let k=1;k<line.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(line[k][0]+dx, line[k][1]+dy);
          ctx.stroke();
        }

        ctx.restore();
      }
    }

    // 暗角（讓日夜更替更明顯）
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(
      W*0.5, H*0.42, Math.min(W,H)*0.18,
      W*0.5, H*0.5,  Math.min(W,H)*0.95
    );
    vig.addColorStop(0, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    vig.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,${(0.18 + 0.42*night)*alpha})`);
    ctx.fillStyle = vig;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  }

  // ---------- Corridor ----------
  function drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, flow, moveStrength, sky, alpha=1){
    const topY = sunY + Math.min(W,H)*0.04;
    const botY = H*1.02;

    const topW = W*0.12;
    const botW = W*0.90;
    const cx = sunX;

    const x1t = cx - topW*0.5, x2t = cx + topW*0.5;
    const x1b = cx - botW*0.5, x2b = cx + botW*0.5;

    const baseA = mixRGB([140,240,255],[255,84,214],0.25);
    const baseB = mixRGB([60,120,255],[0,0,0],0.08);

    const grd = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, topY, 0, botY);
    grd.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(mixRGB(baseA, sky, 0.18), 0.50*alpha));
    grd.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(mixRGB(baseB, sky, 0.12), 0.88*alpha));

    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(x1t, topY); ctx.lineTo(x2t, topY);
    ctx.lineTo(x2b, botY); ctx.lineTo(x1b, botY);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.clip();

    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.84;
    ctx.fillStyle = grd;
    ctx.fillRect(0, topY, W, botY-topY);

    const speed = lerp(0.0, 1.0, moveStrength);
    const stripeOffset = (flow * 260 * speed) % 96;

    for(let i=-4;i<30;i++){
      const y = topY + i*34 + stripeOffset;
      const t = clamp((y-topY)/(botY-topY),0,1);
      const halfW = lerp(topW*0.55, botW*0.55, smooth(t));
      const xl = cx-halfW, xr=cx+halfW;

      const cfg = STATE.ridges[(i+100)%STATE.ridges.length];
      const col = hexToRgb(cfg.stops[1]);
      const stripeCol = mixRGB([255,255,255], col, 0.30);

      const a = lerp(0.26, 0.06, t) * alpha;
      ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(stripeCol, a);
      ctx.lineWidth = lerp(1.8, 1.0, t);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(xl,y); ctx.lineTo(xr,y); ctx.stroke();
    }

    ctx.restore();

    const holeR = Math.min(W,H)*0.22;
    const hole = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, topY, 0, cx, topY, holeR);
    hole.addColorStop(0, `rgba(16,14,22,${0.62*alpha})`);
    hole.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle = hole;
    ctx.fillRect(cx-holeR, topY-holeR, holeR*2, holeR*2);
  }

  // ---------- Sun (永遠最後畫) ----------
  function drawSun(x,y,r,color,glow=1,alpha=1){
    const R = r*(7*glow);
    const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
    g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(color, 0.26*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(0.22, rgbStr(lighten(color,0.10), 0.16*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(color, 0.98*alpha); ctx.fill();

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x-r*0.22,y-r*0.22,r*0.35,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${0.36*alpha})`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // ---------- Layer 3: Space ----------
  function drawSpace(alpha=1){
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(5,6,12,${alpha})`;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    const neb=ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.35,H*0.35,0, W*0.35,H*0.35, Math.min(W,H)*0.9);
    neb.addColorStop(0, `rgba(120,90,255,${0.10*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(0.5, `rgba(80,220,255,${0.05*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=neb;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    for(let i=0;i<140;i++){
      const x=(hash2(i,9.1)*W), y=(hash2(i,2.7)*H);
      const a=(hash2(i,6.3)*0.06+0.01)*alpha;
      const r=hash2(i,4.2)*1.2+0.2;
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }

    for(const s of stars){
      const x=s.x*W, y=s.y*H;
      const tw=(Math.sin(time*1.6+s.twSeed)*0.5+0.5);
      const a=lerp(0.35,0.95,tw)*alpha;

      const R=s.r*10;
      const g=ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
      g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(s.color, 0.24*a));
      g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
      ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

      ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(s.color,a);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,s.r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }
  }

  // ---------- Update / Render ----------
  function update(dt){
    time += dt;

    // zoom inertia
    zoomVel *= 0.84;
    zoom = clamp(zoom - zoomVel, 0, 1);

    // 日夜更替（明顯）
    timeDay = (timeDay + dt*0.05) % 1;
    const sky = skyAt(timeDay);

    const inTerrain = (zoom > 0.45);
    const wantsMove = pointer.down && !inColorize && inTerrain;

    // 前進（按住才會加速）
    const targetVel = wantsMove ? 1 : 0;
    travelVel += (targetVel - travelVel) * (1 - Math.pow(0.001, dt));
    travel += travelVel * dt * 1.55;

    // 追光距離
    if(!inColorize){
      if(wantsMove) reach -= dt*0.62;
      else          reach += dt*0.08;
      reach = clamp(reach,0,1);

      if(reach <= 0.04){
        inColorize=true;
        colorizeT=0;
        pendingColor=randomDreamColor();
      }
    } else {
      colorizeT += dt*1.15;
      if(colorizeT >= 1){
        addStar(pendingColor);
        sun.curColor = sun.baseColor.slice();
        inColorize=false;
        reach=1;
      } else {
        const t=colorizeT;
        const up = t<0.55 ? smooth(t/0.55) : smooth((1-t)/0.45);
        sun.curColor = mixRGB(sun.baseColor, pendingColor, up);
      }
    }

    render(sky);
  }

  function render(sky){
    const layer = currentLayer();
    const terrainAlpha = clamp((zoom - 0.35)/0.65, 0, 1);
    const spaceAlpha = 1 - terrainAlpha;

    if(spaceAlpha>0.001) drawSpace(spaceAlpha);

    if(terrainAlpha>0.001){
      const flow = travel*2.45;

      // 1) terrain
      drawMultiRidgeTerrain(sky, flow, terrainAlpha);

      const sunX = W*(sun.x + Math.sin(time*0.20)*0.002);
      const sunY = H*(sun.y + Math.cos(time*0.16)*0.002);

      // 2) corridor overlay
      drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, travel, travelVel, sky, terrainAlpha);

      // 3) layer2 colorize overlay
      if(inColorize){
        const t=smooth(colorizeT);
        const flashA = lerp(0.00,0.30, Math.sin(Math.PI*t));
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${flashA*terrainAlpha})`;
        ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

        const baseR = Math.min(W,H)*0.018;
        const ringR = lerp(baseR*2.2, Math.min(W,H)*0.36, t);
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(sunX,sunY,ringR,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(pendingColor, 0.48*terrainAlpha);
        ctx.lineWidth = lerp(2.8,1.0,t);
        ctx.stroke();
      }

      // 4) sun LAST (保證可見)
      const baseR = Math.min(W,H)*0.018;
      const grow = lerp(1.0, 3.1, smooth(1-reach));
      const pulse = (Math.sin(time*1.2)*0.5+0.5);
      const glow  = lerp(1.0, 2.1, smooth(1-reach));
      drawSun(sunX, sunY, baseR*grow*(1.0+pulse*0.05), sun.curColor, glow, terrainAlpha);

      // hint
      if(!pointer.down && !inColorize){
        const a=(Math.sin(time*2.0)*0.5+0.5)*0.35*terrainAlpha;
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
        ctx.font=`600 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.018))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
        ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
        ctx.fillText('按住左鍵追光前進', W*0.5, H*0.82);
      }
    }

    // HUD
    pillLayer.textContent = `layer: ${inColorize ? '2' : layer}`;
    pillStars.textContent = `stars: ${stars.length}`;
    pillZoom.textContent  = `zoom: ${zoom.toFixed(2)}`;
    pillTime.textContent  = `time: ${Math.round(timeDay*100)}%`;

    if(layer===3 && !inColorize){
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.55)`;
      ctx.font=`500 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.016))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
      ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
      ctx.fillText('滾輪放大回到地勢圖（第一層）', W*0.5, H*0.90);
      if(stars.length===0){
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.42)`;
        ctx.fillText('宇宙尚未生成繁星：先回去追光並完成染色', W*0.5, H*0.84);
      }
    }
  }

  // ---------- Loop ----------
  let last=performance.now();
  function loop(now){
    const dt=Math.min(0.033,(now-last)/1000);
    last=now;
    update(dt);
    requestAnimationFrame(loop);
  }
  requestAnimationFrame(loop);

  // =========================
  // Panel UI (後台)
  // =========================
  const panelBody = document.getElementById('panelBody');
  const btnToggle = document.getElementById('btnToggle');
  const panel = document.getElementById('panel');

  let collapsed=false;
  btnToggle.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
    collapsed=!collapsed;
    panelBody.style.display = collapsed ? 'none' : 'block';
    btnToggle.textContent = collapsed ? '展開' : '收合';
  });

  function mkRow(labelText, inputEl){
    const row=document.createElement('div');
    row.className='row';
    const label=document.createElement('label');
    label.textContent=labelText;
    row.appendChild(label);
    row.appendChild(inputEl);
    return row;
  }
  function mkRange(min,max,step,value,oninput){
    const r=document.createElement('input');
    r.type='range'; r.min=min; r.max=max; r.step=step; r.value=value;
    r.addEventListener('input', ()=>oninput(parseFloat(r.value)));
    return r;
  }
  function mkColor(value,oninput){
    const c=document.createElement('input');
    c.type='color'; c.value=value;
    c.addEventListener('input', ()=>oninput(c.value));
    return c;
  }
  function mkBtn(text, fn){
    const b=document.createElement('button');
    b.className='btn';
    b.textContent=text;
    b.addEventListener('click', fn);
    return b;
  }

  function renderPanel(){
    panelBody.innerHTML='';

    // Global
    const g = STATE.global;
    const gBox=document.createElement('div');
    gBox.className='group';
    const gt=document.createElement('div');
    gt.className='groupTop';
    gt.innerHTML = `<span class="tag">Global</span><span class="tag">手繪筆觸＋層數</span>`;
    gBox.appendChild(gt);

    gBox.appendChild(mkRow('layers', mkRange(1, STATE.ridges.length, 1, g.layers, v=>g.layers=v)));
    gBox.appendChild(mkRow('line',   mkRange(1, 8, 0.1, g.lineWidth, v=>g.lineWidth=v)));
    gBox.appendChild(mkRow('fill',   mkRange(0, 0.6, 0.01, g.fillAlpha, v=>g.fillAlpha=v)));
    gBox.appendChild(mkRow('jitter', mkRange(0, 6, 0.1, g.handJitter, v=>g.handJitter=v)));
    gBox.appendChild(mkRow('wobble', mkRange(0, 3, 0.1, g.handWobble, v=>g.handWobble=v)));
    gBox.appendChild(mkRow('cont#',  mkRange(1, 7, 1, g.multiContours, v=>g.multiContours=v)));
    gBox.appendChild(mkRow('space',  mkRange(0.5, 6, 0.1, g.contourSpacing, v=>g.contourSpacing=v)));

    const sketchRow=document.createElement('div');
    sketchRow.className='row';
    const lb=document.createElement('label'); lb.textContent='double';
    const cb=document.createElement('input'); cb.type='checkbox'; cb.checked=g.sketchDouble;
    cb.addEventListener('change', ()=>g.sketchDouble=cb.checked);
    sketchRow.appendChild(lb); sketchRow.appendChild(cb);
    gBox.appendChild(sketchRow);

    panelBody.appendChild(gBox);

    // Ridges
    STATE.ridges.forEach((r, idx)=>{
      const box=document.createElement('div');
      box.className='group';

      const top=document.createElement('div');
      top.className='groupTop';
      top.innerHTML = `<span class="tag">ridge ${idx+1}: ${r.name}</span><span class="tag">ramp / amp / speed</span>`;
      box.appendChild(top);

      // ramp colors (3 stops)
      const rampRow=document.createElement('div');
      rampRow.className='row';
      const lab=document.createElement('label');
      lab.textContent='ramp';
      rampRow.appendChild(lab);
      const c0=mkColor(r.stops[0], v=>r.stops[0]=v);
      const c1=mkColor(r.stops[1], v=>r.stops[1]=v);
      const c2=mkColor(r.stops[2], v=>r.stops[2]=v);
      rampRow.appendChild(c0); rampRow.appendChild(c1); rampRow.appendChild(c2);
      box.appendChild(rampRow);

      box.appendChild(mkRow('amp',   mkRange(20, 220, 1, r.amp, v=>r.amp=v)));
      box.appendChild(mkRow('speed', mkRange(0.2, 3.0, 0.05, r.speed, v=>r.speed=v)));
      box.appendChild(mkRow('thick', mkRange(10, 120, 1, r.thick, v=>r.thick=v)));

      panelBody.appendChild(box);
    });

    // Export / Import
    const io=document.createElement('div');
    io.className='group';
    const iot=document.createElement('div');
    iot.className='groupTop';
    iot.innerHTML=`<span class="tag">Export / Import</span><span class="tag">後台 JSON</span>`;
    io.appendChild(iot);

    const ta=document.createElement('textarea');
    ta.value = JSON.stringify(STATE, null, 2);
    io.appendChild(ta);

    const btns=document.createElement('div');
    btns.className='miniBtns';

    btns.appendChild(mkBtn('更新為當前設定', ()=>{ ta.value = JSON.stringify(STATE, null, 2); }));
    btns.appendChild(mkBtn('套用 JSON', ()=>{
      try{
        const obj = JSON.parse(ta.value);
        if(!obj || !obj.ridges || !obj.global) throw new Error('JSON 格式不對');
        // 最小防呆：只覆蓋允許的欄位
        STATE.global = { ...STATE.global, ...obj.global };
        STATE.ridges = obj.ridges.map((r,i)=>({
          name: r.name ?? (`ridge${i+1}`),
          amp:  Number(r.amp ?? 100),
          speed:Number(r.speed ?? 1),
          thick:Number(r.thick ?? 50),
          seed: Number(r.seed ?? (10+i*7)),
          stops: Array.isArray(r.stops) ? [
            r.stops[0] ?? "#ffffff",
            r.stops[1] ?? "#ffffff",
            r.stops[2] ?? "#ffffff"
          ] : ["#ffffff","#ffffff","#ffffff"],
        }));
        renderPanel();
      }catch(err){
        alert('套用失敗：' + err.message);
      }
    }));

    io.appendChild(btns);
    const hint=document.createElement('div');
    hint.className='hint';
    hint.textContent='你可以把 JSON 存檔當後台資料；之後貼回來按「套用 JSON」就會復原顏色 ramp。';
    io.appendChild(hint);

    panelBody.appendChild(io);
  }

  renderPanel();
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
你現在能做到的事（不用改程式）

在左下角面板直接改每條線的 3 段 ramp（像 TD 的 3 stops）

調整每條的 amp / speed / thick → 起伏更大、流更快、山帶更厚

調整全域的 handJitter / multiContours / contourSpacing → 更像手繪線、更像等高線堆疊

用 Export/Import JSON：把 ramp 設定當成「後台資料」保存/載入

如果你想要更像 TouchDesigner 的 ramp（5 個 stops 或 可加/刪 stops），我也可以把面板升級成「動態 stops（+ / -）」版本。你只要說你希望每條最多幾個 stops（5？7？）。



你說：
我不想要讓那個可以調整的UI直接出現在網頁上 拿掉好了 我自己在後台調就好


ChatGPT 說：

OK，我把「可調 UI 面板」整個拿掉，只保留 後台可調的 JSON（STATE）。你之後要改 ramp / amp / speed / thick，就直接改 STATE 裡面的數值即可。

下面是最新整合版（無 UI）：保留三層、互動、追光、染色記錄成星星、滾輪進出宇宙、日夜更替、以及手繪筆觸＋多條繽紛山河線（每條獨立起伏/速度/ramp）。

請把整份 HTML 覆蓋成這份。

HTML
<!doctype html>

  <style>

<body>
  <div id="wrap"><canvas id="c"></canvas></div>

  <div class="hud">
    <div><b>操作</b>：左鍵按住前進｜放開停止｜滾輪縮小進宇宙｜滾輪放大回地勢</div>
    <div class="muted">抵達亮點 → 自動染色 → 記錄成宇宙繁星（第三層）。</div>
    <div class="pillrow">
      <div class="pill" id="pillLayer">layer: 1</div>
      <div class="pill" id="pillStars">stars: 0</div>
      <div class="pill" id="pillZoom">zoom: 1.00</div>
      <div class="pill" id="pillTime">time: 0%</div>
    </div>

<script>
(() => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('c');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', { alpha:false });

  const pillLayer = document.getElementById('pillLayer');
  const pillStars = document.getElementById('pillStars');
  const pillZoom  = document.getElementById('pillZoom');
  const pillTime  = document.getElementById('pillTime');

  // =========================================================
  // BACKEND（你自己在後台調整就改這裡）
  // - 每條 ridge 有自己的起伏 amp、速度 speed、厚度 thick、顏色 ramp stops
  // - stops 建議 3 個（上/中/下），會做成每層自己的縱向漸層
  // =========================================================
  const STATE = {
    ridges: [
      { name:"blue",   amp:130, speed:1.7, thick:70, seed:11, stops:["#2f66ff","#6ff7ff","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"pink",   amp:115, speed:1.2, thick:62, seed:23, stops:["#ff4fd8","#ffd2ff","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"orange", amp:105, speed:1.45,thick:56, seed:37, stops:["#ff8a3d","#ffe36a","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"violet", amp:120, speed:1.05,thick:64, seed:47, stops:["#8a5bff","#ff7fd6","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"green",  amp:100, speed:1.15,thick:50, seed:59, stops:["#39ff88","#c8ff5b","#ffffff"] },
    ],
    global: {
      layers: 5,
      lineWidth: 3.2,
      contourAlpha: 0.95,
      fillAlpha: 0.18,

      // 手繪筆觸
      handJitter: 2.2,      // 抖動強度(px)
      handWobble: 0.9,      // 流動擺動強度
      multiContours: 3,     // 主線+副線總數
      contourSpacing: 2.2,  // 副線間距(px)
      sketchDouble: true,   // 雙描線
    }
  };

  // ---------- Responsive ----------
  let W=0,H=0,dpr=1;
  function resize(){
    dpr = Math.max(1, Math.min(2, window.devicePixelRatio || 1));
    W = Math.floor(window.innerWidth);
    H = Math.floor(window.innerHeight);
    canvas.width = Math.floor(W*dpr);
    canvas.height= Math.floor(H*dpr);
    canvas.style.width = W+'px';
    canvas.style.height= H+'px';
    ctx.setTransform(dpr,0,0,dpr,0,0);
  }
  window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
  resize();

  // ---------- Utils ----------
  const clamp=(v,a,b)=>Math.max(a,Math.min(b,v));
  const lerp=(a,b,t)=>a+(b-a)*t;
  const smooth=(t)=>t*t*(3-2*t);
  const fract=(x)=>x-Math.floor(x);

  function hash2(x,y){
    const s = Math.sin(x*127.1 + y*311.7) * 43758.5453123;
    return fract(s);
  }
  function valueNoise(x,y){
    const xi=Math.floor(x), yi=Math.floor(y);
    const xf=x-xi, yf=y-yi;
    const a=hash2(xi,yi), b=hash2(xi+1,yi);
    const c=hash2(xi,yi+1), d=hash2(xi+1,yi+1);
    const u=smooth(xf), v=smooth(yf);
    return lerp(lerp(a,b,u), lerp(c,d,u), v);
  }
  function fbm(x,y){
    let f=0, amp=0.62, freq=1.0;
    for(let i=0;i<5;i++){
      f += amp * valueNoise(x*freq, y*freq);
      freq *= 2.0;
      amp *= 0.52;
    }
    return f;
  }
  function hexToRgb(hex){
    const h = hex.replace('#','').trim();
    const v = parseInt(h.length===3 ? h.split('').map(c=>c+c).join('') : h, 16);
    return [(v>>16)&255, (v>>8)&255, v&255];
  }
  function mixRGB(a,b,t){
    return [Math.round(lerp(a[0],b[0],t)), Math.round(lerp(a[1],b[1],t)), Math.round(lerp(a[2],b[2],t))];
  }
  function rgbStr(c,a=1){ return `rgba(${c[0]},${c[1]},${c[2]},${a})`; }
  function darken(c,t){ return mixRGB(c,[0,0,0],t); }
  function lighten(c,t){ return mixRGB(c,[255,255,255],t); }

  // ---------- Input ----------
  const pointer = {x:0,y:0,down:false};
  window.addEventListener('pointerdown',(e)=>{
    if(e.button!==0) return;
    pointer.down=true;
    pointer.x=e.clientX; pointer.y=e.clientY;
  });
  window.addEventListener('pointerup',(e)=>{
    if(e.button!==0) return;
    pointer.down=false;
  });
  window.addEventListener('pointermove',(e)=>{
    pointer.x=e.clientX; pointer.y=e.clientY;
  });

  let zoom=1.0, zoomVel=0;
  window.addEventListener('wheel',(e)=>{
    e.preventDefault();
    zoomVel += Math.sign(e.deltaY) * 0.06;
  }, {passive:false});

  // ---------- State ----------
  let time=0;
  let timeDay=0;        // 0..1
  let travel=0;
  let travelVel=0;
  let reach=1;

  let inColorize=false;
  let colorizeT=0;
  let pendingColor=[255,140,220];

  const sun={ x:0.5, y:0.44, baseColor:[255,246,222], curColor:[255,246,222] };

  const stars=[];
  function addStar(color){
    const cx=sun.x+(Math.random()-0.5)*0.12;
    const cy=sun.y+(Math.random()-0.5)*0.12;
    stars.push({ x:clamp(cx,0.06,0.94), y:clamp(cy,0.06,0.94), r:lerp(0.9,2.8,Math.random()), color, twSeed:Math.random()*1000 });
  }

  // ---------- Sky (日夜) ----------
  const skyStops=[
    {t:0.00, c:[252,252,255]},
    {t:0.33, c:[255,214,195]},
    {t:0.66, c:[34, 86, 195]},
    {t:1.00, c:[10, 12, 20]},
  ];
  function skyAt(t){
    t=clamp(t,0,1);
    for(let i=0;i<skyStops.length-1;i++){
      const a=skyStops[i], b=skyStops[i+1];
      if(t>=a.t && t<=b.t){
        const u=smooth((t-a.t)/(b.t-a.t));
        return mixRGB(a.c,b.c,u);
      }
    }
    return skyStops[skyStops.length-1].c;
  }
  function nightAmount(t){
    const n = clamp((t-0.58)/0.25, 0, 1);
    return smooth(n);
  }

  function currentLayer(){ return (zoom<0.45)?3:1; }

  function randomDreamColor(){
    const choices=[[255,80,200],[80,240,255],[255,230,80],[170,120,255],[120,255,170],[255,140,110]];
    const a=choices[(Math.random()*choices.length)|0];
    const b=choices[(Math.random()*choices.length)|0];
    return mixRGB(a,b,Math.random()*0.85);
  }

  // ==========================================
  // Layer 1: 多層山河（每層獨立）＋手繪筆觸
  // ==========================================
  function drawMultiRidgeTerrain(sky, flow, alpha=1){
    // SKY
    const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
    g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(lighten(sky,0.10), alpha));
    g.addColorStop(0.55, rgbStr(sky, alpha));
    g.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(darken(sky,0.32), alpha));
    ctx.fillStyle=g;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    const night = nightAmount(timeDay);

    // 夜晚星塵
    if(night > 0.02){
      for(let i=0;i<160;i++){
        const x = hash2(i, 9.1)*W;
        const y = hash2(i, 2.7)*H*0.65;
        const a = (hash2(i, 6.3)*0.10 + 0.02) * night * alpha;
        const r = hash2(i, 4.2)*1.2 + 0.2;
        ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
      }
    }

    const horizon = H*0.18;
    const depthEnd = H*0.96;

    const G = STATE.global;
    const ridges = STATE.ridges;
    const layers = Math.min(G.layers, ridges.length);
    const stepX = Math.max(6, Math.floor(W/210));

    // 每層基準高度：拉開
    const baseY = [];
    for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
      const t = i/(layers-1 || 1);
      baseY.push(lerp(horizon + H*0.06, depthEnd - H*0.10, t));
    }

    // ---- fill bands ----
    for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
      const cfg = ridges[i];
      const y0 = baseY[i];
      const y1 = (i<layers-1) ? baseY[i+1] : depthEnd + H*0.12;

      const top=[], bot=[];
      for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
        const nx = (x - W*0.5) * 0.00215;
        const f  = flow * 0.22 * cfg.speed;

        const n  = fbm(nx + cfg.seed,        i*1.7 + f);
        const n2 = fbm(nx*1.55 + cfg.seed*2, i*2.1 + f*0.7);
        const h  = (n*0.65 + n2*0.35 - 0.5);

        const persp = lerp(0.70, 1.45, i/(layers-1 || 1));
        const amp = cfg.amp * persp;

        const jitter = (hash2(x*0.05, i*33.3) - 0.5) * G.handJitter;
        const wob = Math.sin((x*0.012) + time*0.6 + i*1.3) * G.handWobble;

        top.push([x, y0 + h*amp + jitter + wob]);
        bot.push([x, y1 + h*amp*0.35 + cfg.thick + jitter*0.35]);
      }

      // ramp: 3 stops（上/中/下）
      const c0 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[0]), sky, 0.10);
      const c1 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[1]), sky, 0.10);
      const c2 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[2]), sky, 0.10);

      const fillG = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, y0, 0, y1);
      fillG.addColorStop(0,   rgbStr(c0,1));
      fillG.addColorStop(0.5, rgbStr(c1,1));
      fillG.addColorStop(1,   rgbStr(c2,1));

      ctx.save();
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(top[0][0], top[0][1]);
      for(let k=1;k<top.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(top[k][0], top[k][1]);
      for(let k=bot.length-1;k>=0;k--) ctx.lineTo(bot[k][0], bot[k][1]);
      ctx.closePath();
      ctx.globalAlpha = G.fillAlpha * alpha;
      ctx.fillStyle = fillG;
      ctx.fill();
      ctx.restore();
    }

    // ---- contour lines (multi) ----
    for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
      const cfg = ridges[i];
      const y0 = baseY[i];

      const line=[];
      for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
        const nx = (x - W*0.5) * 0.00215;
        const f  = flow * 0.22 * cfg.speed;

        const n  = fbm(nx + cfg.seed,        i*1.7 + f);
        const n2 = fbm(nx*1.55 + cfg.seed*2, i*2.1 + f*0.7);
        const h  = (n*0.65 + n2*0.35 - 0.5);

        const persp = lerp(0.70, 1.45, i/(layers-1 || 1));
        const amp = cfg.amp * persp;

        const jitter = (hash2(x*0.05, i*33.3+9.9) - 0.5) * G.handJitter;
        const wob = Math.sin((x*0.012) + time*0.6 + i*1.3) * G.handWobble;

        line.push([x, y0 + h*amp + jitter + wob]);
      }

      // 線沿線漸層（更繽紛）
      const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, y0, W, y0);
      grad.addColorStop(0,   cfg.stops[0]);
      grad.addColorStop(0.5, cfg.stops[1]);
      grad.addColorStop(1,   cfg.stops[2]);

      const mainAlpha = G.contourAlpha * alpha;
      const count = Math.max(1, Math.floor(G.multiContours));
      const spacing = G.contourSpacing;
      const mid = Math.floor((count-1)/2);

      for(let ci=0; ci<count; ci++){
        const off = (ci - mid) * spacing;

        ctx.save();
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(line[0][0], line[0][1] + off);
        for(let k=1;k<line.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(line[k][0], line[k][1] + off);

        ctx.lineJoin="round"; ctx.lineCap="round";
        ctx.globalAlpha = (ci===mid ? mainAlpha : mainAlpha*0.35);
        ctx.strokeStyle = grad;
        ctx.lineWidth = (ci===mid ? G.lineWidth : Math.max(1.1, G.lineWidth*0.62));
        ctx.stroke();

        // 外發光
        ctx.globalAlpha = (ci===mid ? 0.18 : 0.10) * alpha;
        ctx.strokeStyle = cfg.stops[1];
        ctx.lineWidth = (ci===mid ? G.lineWidth*2.7 : G.lineWidth*2.0);
        ctx.stroke();

        // 手繪雙描線（主線才做）
        if(G.sketchDouble && ci===mid){
          const dx = (hash2(i*9.7, 1.3)-0.5)*1.4;
          const dy = (hash2(i*9.7, 8.1)-0.5)*1.4;
          ctx.globalAlpha = 0.22 * alpha;
          ctx.strokeStyle = cfg.stops[0];
          ctx.lineWidth = Math.max(1.2, G.lineWidth*0.95);
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(line[0][0]+dx, line[0][1]+dy);
          for(let k=1;k<line.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(line[k][0]+dx, line[k][1]+dy);
          ctx.stroke();
        }

        ctx.restore();
      }
    }

    // 暗角
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(
      W*0.5, H*0.42, Math.min(W,H)*0.18,
      W*0.5, H*0.5,  Math.min(W,H)*0.95
    );
    vig.addColorStop(0, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    vig.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,${(0.18 + 0.42*night)*alpha})`);
    ctx.fillStyle = vig;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  }

  // ---------- Corridor ----------
  function drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, flow, moveStrength, sky, alpha=1){
    const topY = sunY + Math.min(W,H)*0.04;
    const botY = H*1.02;

    const topW = W*0.12;
    const botW = W*0.90;
    const cx = sunX;

    const x1t = cx - topW*0.5, x2t = cx + topW*0.5;
    const x1b = cx - botW*0.5, x2b = cx + botW*0.5;

    const baseA = mixRGB([140,240,255],[255,84,214],0.25);
    const baseB = mixRGB([60,120,255],[0,0,0],0.08);

    const grd = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, topY, 0, botY);
    grd.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(mixRGB(baseA, sky, 0.18), 0.50*alpha));
    grd.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(mixRGB(baseB, sky, 0.12), 0.88*alpha));

    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(x1t, topY); ctx.lineTo(x2t, topY);
    ctx.lineTo(x2b, botY); ctx.lineTo(x1b, botY);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.clip();

    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.84;
    ctx.fillStyle = grd;
    ctx.fillRect(0, topY, W, botY-topY);

    const speed = lerp(0.0, 1.0, moveStrength);
    const stripeOffset = (flow * 260 * speed) % 96;

    for(let i=-4;i<30;i++){
      const y = topY + i*34 + stripeOffset;
      const t = clamp((y-topY)/(botY-topY),0,1);
      const halfW = lerp(topW*0.55, botW*0.55, smooth(t));
      const xl = cx-halfW, xr=cx+halfW;

      const cfg = STATE.ridges[(i+100)%STATE.ridges.length];
      const col = hexToRgb(cfg.stops[1]);
      const stripeCol = mixRGB([255,255,255], col, 0.30);

      const a = lerp(0.26, 0.06, t) * alpha;
      ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(stripeCol, a);
      ctx.lineWidth = lerp(1.8, 1.0, t);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(xl,y); ctx.lineTo(xr,y); ctx.stroke();
    }

    ctx.restore();

    const holeR = Math.min(W,H)*0.22;
    const hole = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, topY, 0, cx, topY, holeR);
    hole.addColorStop(0, `rgba(16,14,22,${0.62*alpha})`);
    hole.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle = hole;
    ctx.fillRect(cx-holeR, topY-holeR, holeR*2, holeR*2);
  }

  // ---------- Sun (永遠最後畫) ----------
  function drawSun(x,y,r,color,glow=1,alpha=1){
    const R = r*(7*glow);
    const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
    g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(color, 0.26*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(0.22, rgbStr(lighten(color,0.10), 0.16*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(color, 0.98*alpha); ctx.fill();

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x-r*0.22,y-r*0.22,r*0.35,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${0.36*alpha})`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // ---------- Layer 3: Space ----------
  function drawSpace(alpha=1){
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(5,6,12,${alpha})`;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    const neb=ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.35,H*0.35,0, W*0.35,H*0.35, Math.min(W,H)*0.9);
    neb.addColorStop(0, `rgba(120,90,255,${0.10*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(0.5, `rgba(80,220,255,${0.05*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=neb;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    for(let i=0;i<140;i++){
      const x=(hash2(i,9.1)*W), y=(hash2(i,2.7)*H);
      const a=(hash2(i,6.3)*0.06+0.01)*alpha;
      const r=hash2(i,4.2)*1.2+0.2;
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }

    for(const s of stars){
      const x=s.x*W, y=s.y*H;
      const tw=(Math.sin(time*1.6+s.twSeed)*0.5+0.5);
      const a=lerp(0.35,0.95,tw)*alpha;

      const R=s.r*10;
      const g=ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
      g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(s.color, 0.24*a));
      g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
      ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

      ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(s.color,a);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,s.r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }
  }

  // ---------- Update / Render ----------
  function update(dt){
    time += dt;

    zoomVel *= 0.84;
    zoom = clamp(zoom - zoomVel, 0, 1);

    timeDay = (timeDay + dt*0.05) % 1;
    const sky = skyAt(timeDay);

    const inTerrain = (zoom > 0.45);
    const wantsMove = pointer.down && !inColorize && inTerrain;

    const targetVel = wantsMove ? 1 : 0;
    travelVel += (targetVel - travelVel) * (1 - Math.pow(0.001, dt));
    travel += travelVel * dt * 1.55;

    if(!inColorize){
      if(wantsMove) reach -= dt*0.62;
      else          reach += dt*0.08;
      reach = clamp(reach,0,1);

      if(reach <= 0.04){
        inColorize=true;
        colorizeT=0;
        pendingColor=randomDreamColor();
      }
    } else {
      colorizeT += dt*1.15;
      if(colorizeT >= 1){
        addStar(pendingColor);
        sun.curColor = sun.baseColor.slice();
        inColorize=false;
        reach=1;
      } else {
        const t=colorizeT;
        const up = t<0.55 ? smooth(t/0.55) : smooth((1-t)/0.45);
        sun.curColor = mixRGB(sun.baseColor, pendingColor, up);
      }
    }

    render(sky);
  }

  function render(sky){
    const layer = currentLayer();
    const terrainAlpha = clamp((zoom - 0.35)/0.65, 0, 1);
    const spaceAlpha = 1 - terrainAlpha;

    if(spaceAlpha>0.001) drawSpace(spaceAlpha);

    if(terrainAlpha>0.001){
      const flow = travel*2.45;

      drawMultiRidgeTerrain(sky, flow, terrainAlpha);

      const sunX = W*(sun.x + Math.sin(time*0.20)*0.002);
      const sunY = H*(sun.y + Math.cos(time*0.16)*0.002);

      drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, travel, travelVel, sky, terrainAlpha);

      if(inColorize){
        const t=smooth(colorizeT);
        const flashA = lerp(0.00,0.30, Math.sin(Math.PI*t));
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${flashA*terrainAlpha})`;
        ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

        const baseR = Math.min(W,H)*0.018;
        const ringR = lerp(baseR*2.2, Math.min(W,H)*0.36, t);
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(sunX,sunY,ringR,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(pendingColor, 0.48*terrainAlpha);
        ctx.lineWidth = lerp(2.8,1.0,t);
        ctx.stroke();
      }

      const baseR = Math.min(W,H)*0.018;
      const grow = lerp(1.0, 3.1, smooth(1-reach));
      const pulse = (Math.sin(time*1.2)*0.5+0.5);
      const glow  = lerp(1.0, 2.1, smooth(1-reach));
      drawSun(sunX, sunY, baseR*grow*(1.0+pulse*0.05), sun.curColor, glow, terrainAlpha);

      if(!pointer.down && !inColorize){
        const a=(Math.sin(time*2.0)*0.5+0.5)*0.35*terrainAlpha;
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
        ctx.font=`600 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.018))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
        ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
        ctx.fillText('按住左鍵追光前進', W*0.5, H*0.82);
      }
    }

    pillLayer.textContent = `layer: ${inColorize ? '2' : layer}`;
    pillStars.textContent = `stars: ${stars.length}`;
    pillZoom.textContent  = `zoom: ${zoom.toFixed(2)}`;
    pillTime.textContent  = `time: ${Math.round(timeDay*100)}%`;

    if(layer===3 && !inColorize){
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.55)`;
      ctx.font=`500 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.016))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
      ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
      ctx.fillText('滾輪放大回到地勢圖（第一層）', W*0.5, H*0.90);
      if(stars.length===0){
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.42)`;
        ctx.fillText('宇宙尚未生成繁星：先回去追光並完成染色', W*0.5, H*0.84);
      }
    }
  }

  // ---------- Loop ----------
  let last=performance.now();
  function loop(now){
    const dt=Math.min(0.033,(now-last)/1000);
    last=now;
    update(dt);
    requestAnimationFrame(loop);
  }
  requestAnimationFrame(loop);
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
你要怎麼「後台調 ramp」

只要改這段：

JavaScript
stops:["#2f66ff","#6ff7ff","#ffffff"]

stops[0]：上緣（山脊線也會用這些顏色做沿線漸層）

stops[1]：中段

stops[2]：下段

想更像你那張手畫線：把 stops[2] 不要用白，改成更深或更跳的色，層次會更明顯。

如果你也希望連 HUD（左上那個操作提示）都不要出現在作品上，我也可以把 HUD 一起移除（或改成只有 debug 模式才顯示）。



你說：
已上傳一個圖像
我的理想是像這樣好幾層疊起來



ChatGPT 說：

懂，你這張參考圖的關鍵不是「等高線」而是：

每一層都是一整片「山體剪影」（有厚度、像紙片疊起來）

層與層之間有明顯的前後關係：越近越大、越遠越小

每層的顏色是大面積的柔順漸層（不是線條主導）

邊緣要乾淨、圓滑，然後有一點點霧化/柔光

所以我們把地形渲染方式改成：
✅ Silhouette layers（剪影山層）：每層生成一條 top 曲線，然後填到畫面底部；每層都有自己的 ramp（3 stops）與自己的速度/起伏；再加少量柔光與霧。

下面是「直接替換」方案：你不用整份重貼，只要把原本的 drawMultiRidgeTerrain(...) 整個換成這個新版（其他三層/互動/宇宙/亮點都保持不動）。

✅ 替換用：新版剪影山層（像你參考圖那樣疊）

把你現在 HTML 裡的 function drawMultiRidgeTerrain(...) { ... } 整段替換成這個：

JavaScript
function drawMultiRidgeTerrain(sky, flow, alpha=1){
  // SKY（保留日夜）
  const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
  g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(lighten(sky,0.10), alpha));
  g.addColorStop(0.55, rgbStr(sky, alpha));
  g.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(darken(sky,0.32), alpha));
  ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

  const night = nightAmount(timeDay);

  // 夜晚星塵（可見的日夜差異）
  if(night > 0.02){
    for(let i=0;i<120;i++){
      const x = hash2(i, 9.1)*W;
      const y = hash2(i, 2.7)*H*0.65;
      const a = (hash2(i, 6.3)*0.10 + 0.02) * night * alpha;
      const r = hash2(i, 4.2)*1.1 + 0.2;
      ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }
  }

  const G = STATE.global;
  const ridges = STATE.ridges;
  const layers = Math.min(G.layers, ridges.length);

  // 參考圖：遠處山較靠近地平線、近處山更高更大
  const horizon = H*0.46;      // ✅ 讓山體上緣集中在中上（更像圖）
  const bottomY = H*1.05;

  // 畫層：由遠到近（先畫遠的，近的蓋上去）
  for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
    const cfg = ridges[i];
    const t = i/(layers-1 || 1); // 0遠->1近

    // 基準高度：遠的靠上，近的往下（越近山越「大」）
    const baseY = lerp(horizon - H*0.10, H*0.72, smooth(t));

    // 起伏：遠的較小，近的更大（更像疊片）
    const amp = cfg.amp * lerp(0.55, 1.55, smooth(t));

    // 頻率：遠的曲線更平滑，近的細節多一點
    const freq = lerp(0.0014, 0.0025, smooth(t));

    // 流動速度：每層不同
    const f = flow * 0.18 * cfg.speed;

    const stepX = Math.max(8, Math.floor(W/220));
    const pts=[];

    for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
      const nx = (x - W*0.5) * freq;

      // 兩段噪聲混合，曲線更「圓」
      const n  = fbm(nx + cfg.seed,      f + i*3.1);
      const n2 = fbm(nx*1.6 + cfg.seed*2, f*0.75 + i*2.2);
      const h  = (n*0.65 + n2*0.35 - 0.5); // -0.5..0.5

      // 手繪微抖（控制在小幅度，避免鋸齒）
      const jitter = (hash2(x*0.02, i*17.7)-0.5) * (G.handJitter*0.35);
      const wobble = Math.sin(x*0.006 + time*0.55 + i*1.2) * (G.handWobble*0.35);

      pts.push([x, baseY + h*amp + jitter + wobble]);
    }

    // ===== 填色：每層用自己的 ramp（3 stops）=====
    const c0 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[0]), sky, 0.08);
    const c1 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[1]), sky, 0.08);
    const c2 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[2]), sky, 0.08);

    const fillG = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, baseY-amp*0.9, 0, bottomY);
    fillG.addColorStop(0.00, rgbStr(c0, 1));
    fillG.addColorStop(0.55, rgbStr(c1, 1));
    fillG.addColorStop(1.00, rgbStr(c2, 1));

    // ===== 畫剪影山體（像紙片疊）=====
    ctx.save();
    ctx.globalAlpha = alpha; // 直接用 alpha，不要太透明，才有疊片感
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(0, bottomY);
    ctx.lineTo(pts[0][0], pts[0][1]);
    for(let k=1;k<pts.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(pts[k][0], pts[k][1]);
    ctx.lineTo(W, bottomY);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fillStyle = fillG;
    ctx.fill();
    ctx.restore();

    // ===== 柔光邊緣（參考圖的霧感/柔化）=====
    const edgeAlpha = (0.08 + 0.06*(1-t)) * alpha;
    ctx.save();
    ctx.globalAlpha = edgeAlpha;
    ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(lighten(c1, 0.25), 1);
    ctx.lineWidth = lerp(10, 22, 1-t); // 遠處更柔
    ctx.lineJoin="round"; ctx.lineCap="round";
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(pts[0][0], pts[0][1]);
    for(let k=1;k<pts.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(pts[k][0], pts[k][1]);
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.restore();

    // ===== 薄薄的邊線（讓層次更清楚，但不要像等高線）=====
    ctx.save();
    ctx.globalAlpha = (0.10 + 0.10*(1-t)) * alpha;
    ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(lighten(c0, 0.35), 1);
    ctx.lineWidth = lerp(1.1, 2.0, 1-t);
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(pts[0][0], pts[0][1]);
    for(let k=1;k<pts.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(pts[k][0], pts[k][1]);
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.restore();
  }

  // 暗角（夜晚更明顯）
  const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(
    W*0.5, H*0.42, Math.min(W,H)*0.18,
    W*0.5, H*0.5,  Math.min(W,H)*0.95
  );
  vig.addColorStop(0, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
  vig.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,${(0.14 + 0.42*night)*alpha})`);
  ctx.fillStyle = vig;
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

  // 低處霧（讓地面像你參考圖那種白霧漸層）
  const fog = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, H*0.70, 0, H*1.02);
  fog.addColorStop(0, `rgba(255,255,255,0)`);
  fog.addColorStop(1, `rgba(255,255,255,${0.55*alpha})`);
  ctx.fillStyle = fog;
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
}
你會立刻得到的效果

每層仍然有自己的 amp/speed/ramp（你可後台改 STATE.ridges[i].stops）

層次分明、不會融成一體

仍保留你的：通道、亮點、前進、第二層染色、第三層繁星、日夜更替

夜日更替太硬：改成「黑夜慢慢回日」

你現在是用 timeDay = (timeDay + dt*0.05) % 1; 做循環，所以到 1 會瞬間跳回 0（黑→白瞬跳）。
解法：把循環改成「往返的三角波」（0→1→0→1），就會慢慢從夜回日，不會瞬間跳。

✅ 只要改 2 行（推薦）

JavaScript
timeDay = (timeDay + dt*0.05) % 1;
const sky = skyAt(timeDay);

把它換成下面這段：

JavaScript
// 改成往返：0→1→0（避免 1->0 的瞬跳）
timeDay = (timeDay + dt*0.05) % 2;          // 0..2
const tPingPong = timeDay <= 1 ? timeDay : (2 - timeDay); // 0..1..0
const sky = skyAt(tPingPong);

然後把所有用到 timeDay 的地方（例如 nightAmount(timeDay)、HUD 顯示）都改成用 tPingPong。

最簡單做法：在 update(dt) 裡把 tPingPong 存成全域，例如：

JavaScript

JavaScript
timeDay = (timeDay + dt*0.05) % 2;
dayPhase = timeDay <= 1 ? timeDay : (2 - timeDay);
const sky = skyAt(dayPhase);

整體層數/筆觸：STATE.global

ChatGPT 說：

可以。你現在「山河流動」會等到按左鍵才動，是因為地形用的 flow 來源是 travel（只有按住前進才會增加）。
要讓每層 永遠都在流動，但「前進感/通道線條加速/光點靠近」仍然只有按左鍵才發生，我們把 flow 拆成兩個：

ambientFlow（常駐流動）：用 time 來推進，永遠動

travelFlow（前進流動）：仍然用 travel，只有按住才加速，用在通道與靠近感

把它改成：

JavaScript

const terrainFlow = time * 0.55;          // 這個數字越大流動越快
drawMultiRidgeTerrain(sky, terrainFlow, terrainAlpha);

// 2) 通道/前進感仍然跟 travel 走（按住才加速）
drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, travel, travelVel, sky, terrainAlpha);

就這樣。✅

JavaScript
const terrainFlow = time * 0.55 + travel * 0.35;

time * 0.55：常駐流動

+ travel * 0.35：按住時額外推進

🔥 一、加入「永遠流動」變數

🔥 二、修改 update(dt)

找到你現在的 update(dt)，把裡面 flow 相關邏輯改成下面這樣：

JavaScript
function update(dt){
  time += dt;

  // ===== 1️⃣ 永遠流動 =====
  ambientFlow += dt * 0.55;   // 山體自然流動速度（可調）

  // ===== 2️⃣ 滾輪縮放 =====
  zoomVel *= 0.84;
  zoom = clamp(zoom - zoomVel, 0, 1);

  // ===== 3️⃣ 日夜往返（不瞬跳）=====
  timeDay = (timeDay + dt*0.05) % 2;     // 0..2
  dayPhase = timeDay <= 1 ? timeDay : (2 - timeDay);  // 0→1→0

  const sky = skyAt(dayPhase);

  const inTerrain = (zoom > 0.45);
  const wantsMove = pointer.down && !inColorize && inTerrain;

  // ===== 4️⃣ 前進只影響 travel =====
  const targetVel = wantsMove ? 1 : 0;
  travelVel += (targetVel - travelVel) * (1 - Math.pow(0.001, dt));
  travel += travelVel * dt * 1.55;

  // ===== 5️⃣ 抵達亮點 =====
  if(!inColorize){
    if(wantsMove) reach -= dt*0.62;
    else          reach += dt*0.08;

    reach = clamp(reach,0,1);

    if(reach <= 0.04){
      inColorize=true;
      colorizeT=0;
      pendingColor=randomDreamColor();
    }
  } else {
    colorizeT += dt*1.15;
    if(colorizeT >= 1){
      addStar(pendingColor);
      sun.curColor = sun.baseColor.slice();
      inColorize=false;
      reach=1;
    } else {
      const t=colorizeT;
      const up = t<0.55 ? smooth(t/0.55) : smooth((1-t)/0.45);
      sun.curColor = mixRGB(sun.baseColor, pendingColor, up);
    }
  }

  render(sky);
}

<!doctype html>

  <div class="hud">
    <div><b>操作</b>：左鍵按住前進｜放開停止｜滾輪縮小進宇宙｜滾輪放大回地勢</div>

<script>
(() => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('c');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', { alpha:false });

  const pillLayer = document.getElementById('pillLayer');
  const pillStars = document.getElementById('pillStars');
  const pillZoom  = document.getElementById('pillZoom');
  const pillTime  = document.getElementById('pillTime');

  // =========================================================
  // BACKEND（你要調整就改這裡）
  // 每層：stops(3個) / amp / speed / thick
  // =========================================================
  const STATE = {
    ridges: [
      { name:"pink-bg", amp:140, speed:0.9,  thick:80, seed:11, stops:["#ff58c8","#ffd3f0","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"orange",  amp:150, speed:1.05, thick:90, seed:23, stops:["#ff7a22","#ffd46a","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"green",   amp:170, speed:1.10, thick:92, seed:37, stops:["#33ff8a","#cfff6a","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"violet",  amp:165, speed:1.00, thick:96, seed:47, stops:["#8a5bff","#ff7fd6","#ffffff"] },
      { name:"magenta", amp:190, speed:1.15, thick:110,seed:59, stops:["#ff2fb8","#ff8fe6","#ffffff"] },
    ],
    global: {
      layers: 5,

      // 手繪筆觸（剪影邊緣用）
      handJitter: 2.4,
      handWobble: 1.1,

      // 山體填色強度
      fillAlpha: 1.0,

      // 剪影邊緣柔化
      edgeGlow: 0.14,      // 邊緣柔光強度
      edgeWidthNear: 16,   // 近景柔邊厚度
      edgeWidthFar: 26,    // 遠景柔邊厚度

      // 常駐流動速度
      ambientFlowSpeed: 0.55,

      // 按住前進時，山體額外加速（可設 0 代表不加速）
      travelFlowBoost: 0.35,
    }
  };

  // ---------- Responsive ----------
  let W=0,H=0,dpr=1;
  function resize(){
    dpr = Math.max(1, Math.min(2, window.devicePixelRatio || 1));
    W = Math.floor(window.innerWidth);
    H = Math.floor(window.innerHeight);
    canvas.width = Math.floor(W*dpr);
    canvas.height= Math.floor(H*dpr);
    canvas.style.width = W+'px';
    canvas.style.height= H+'px';
    ctx.setTransform(dpr,0,0,dpr,0,0);
  }
  window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
  resize();

  // ---------- Utils ----------
  const clamp=(v,a,b)=>Math.max(a,Math.min(b,v));
  const lerp=(a,b,t)=>a+(b-a)*t;
  const smooth=(t)=>t*t*(3-2*t);
  const fract=(x)=>x-Math.floor(x);

  function hash2(x,y){
    const s = Math.sin(x*127.1 + y*311.7) * 43758.5453123;
    return fract(s);
  }
  function valueNoise(x,y){
    const xi=Math.floor(x), yi=Math.floor(y);
    const xf=x-xi, yf=y-yi;
    const a=hash2(xi,yi), b=hash2(xi+1,yi);
    const c=hash2(xi,yi+1), d=hash2(xi+1,yi+1);
    const u=smooth(xf), v=smooth(yf);
    return lerp(lerp(a,b,u), lerp(c,d,u), v);
  }
  function fbm(x,y){
    let f=0, amp=0.62, freq=1.0;
    for(let i=0;i<5;i++){
      f += amp * valueNoise(x*freq, y*freq);
      freq *= 2.0;
      amp *= 0.52;
    }
    return f;
  }
  function hexToRgb(hex){
    const h = hex.replace('#','').trim();
    const v = parseInt(h.length===3 ? h.split('').map(c=>c+c).join('') : h, 16);
    return [(v>>16)&255, (v>>8)&255, v&255];
  }
  function mixRGB(a,b,t){
    return [Math.round(lerp(a[0],b[0],t)), Math.round(lerp(a[1],b[1],t)), Math.round(lerp(a[2],b[2],t))];
  }
  function rgbStr(c,a=1){ return `rgba(${c[0]},${c[1]},${c[2]},${a})`; }
  function darken(c,t){ return mixRGB(c,[0,0,0],t); }
  function lighten(c,t){ return mixRGB(c,[255,255,255],t); }

  // ---------- Input ----------
  const pointer = {x:0,y:0,down:false};
  window.addEventListener('pointerdown',(e)=>{
    if(e.button!==0) return;
    pointer.down=true;
    pointer.x=e.clientX; pointer.y=e.clientY;
  });
  window.addEventListener('pointerup',(e)=>{
    if(e.button!==0) return;
    pointer.down=false;
  });
  window.addEventListener('pointermove',(e)=>{
    pointer.x=e.clientX; pointer.y=e.clientY;
  });

  let zoom=1.0, zoomVel=0;
  window.addEventListener('wheel',(e)=>{
    e.preventDefault();
    zoomVel += Math.sign(e.deltaY) * 0.06;
  }, {passive:false});

  // ---------- State ----------
  let time=0;

  // 日夜：用往返相位（避免 1->0 硬跳）
  let timeDay=0;     // 0..2
  let dayPhase=0;    // 0..1..0

  // 常駐流動
  let ambientFlow=0;

  // 前進（按住才變）
  let travel=0;
  let travelVel=0;
  let reach=1;

  let inColorize=false;
  let colorizeT=0;
  let pendingColor=[255,140,220];

  const sun={ x:0.5, y:0.44, baseColor:[255,246,222], curColor:[255,246,222] };

  const stars=[];
  function addStar(color){
    const cx=sun.x+(Math.random()-0.5)*0.12;
    const cy=sun.y+(Math.random()-0.5)*0.12;
    stars.push({ x:clamp(cx,0.06,0.94), y:clamp(cy,0.06,0.94), r:lerp(0.9,2.8,Math.random()), color, twSeed:Math.random()*1000 });
  }

  // ---------- Sky (日夜) ----------
  const skyStops=[
    {t:0.00, c:[252,252,255]},
    {t:0.33, c:[255,214,195]},
    {t:0.66, c:[34, 86, 195]},
    {t:1.00, c:[10, 12, 20]},
  ];
  function skyAt(t){
    t=clamp(t,0,1);
    for(let i=0;i<skyStops.length-1;i++){
      const a=skyStops[i], b=skyStops[i+1];
      if(t>=a.t && t<=b.t){
        const u=smooth((t-a.t)/(b.t-a.t));
        return mixRGB(a.c,b.c,u);
      }
    }
    return skyStops[skyStops.length-1].c;
  }
  function nightAmount(t){
    // t: 0..1..0（白天->夜->白天）
    const n = clamp((t-0.58)/0.25, 0, 1);
    return smooth(n);
  }

  function currentLayer(){ return (zoom<0.45)?3:1; }

  function randomDreamColor(){
    const choices=[[255,80,200],[80,240,255],[255,230,80],[170,120,255],[120,255,170],[255,140,110]];
    const a=choices[(Math.random()*choices.length)|0];
    const b=choices[(Math.random()*choices.length)|0];
    return mixRGB(a,b,Math.random()*0.85);
  }

  // ==========================================
  // Layer 1: 剪影疊片山層（像你參考圖那樣）
  // - 每層用 ramp 填色
  // - 每層永遠流動（flow 來自 ambientFlow + 可選 travelBoost）
  // ==========================================
  function drawMultiRidgeTerrainSilhouette(sky, flow, alpha=1){
    // SKY（保留日夜）
    const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
    g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(lighten(sky,0.10), alpha));
    g.addColorStop(0.55, rgbStr(sky, alpha));
    g.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(darken(sky,0.32), alpha));
    ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    const night = nightAmount(dayPhase);

    // 夜晚星塵（讓夜更像夜）
    if(night > 0.02){
      for(let i=0;i<120;i++){
        const x = hash2(i, 9.1)*W;
        const y = hash2(i, 2.7)*H*0.65;
        const a = (hash2(i, 6.3)*0.10 + 0.02) * night * alpha;
        const r = hash2(i, 4.2)*1.1 + 0.2;
        ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
      }
    }

    const G = STATE.global;
    const ridges = STATE.ridges;
    const layers = Math.min(G.layers, ridges.length);

    // 構圖：讓山體集中在中上，底部有霧
    const horizon = H*0.46;
    const bottomY = H*1.06;

    // 由遠到近畫（近景蓋在上面）
    for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
      const cfg = ridges[i];
      const t = i/(layers-1 || 1); // 0遠->1近

      const baseY = lerp(horizon - H*0.12, H*0.72, smooth(t));
      const amp = cfg.amp * lerp(0.55, 1.55, smooth(t));
      const freq = lerp(0.0014, 0.0026, smooth(t));

      const f = flow * 0.18 * cfg.speed;

      const stepX = Math.max(8, Math.floor(W/220));
      const pts=[];

      for(let x=0;x<=W;x+=stepX){
        const nx = (x - W*0.5) * freq;

        const n  = fbm(nx + cfg.seed,        f + i*3.1);
        const n2 = fbm(nx*1.6 + cfg.seed*2,  f*0.75 + i*2.2);
        const h  = (n*0.65 + n2*0.35 - 0.5);

        // 微手繪抖動
        const jitter = (hash2(x*0.02, i*17.7)-0.5) * (G.handJitter*0.35);
        const wobble = Math.sin(x*0.006 + time*0.55 + i*1.2) * (G.handWobble*0.35);

        // valley mask：中間比較空、左右更高（通道更乾淨）
        const mid = x/W - 0.5;
        const valley = 1 - Math.exp(-(mid*mid)/0.05); // 中間小、兩側大
        const sideBoost = lerp(0.85, 1.35, valley);

        pts.push([x, baseY + h*amp*sideBoost + jitter + wobble]);
      }

      // ramp（3 stops）
      const c0 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[0]), sky, 0.06);
      const c1 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[1]), sky, 0.06);
      const c2 = mixRGB(hexToRgb(cfg.stops[2]), sky, 0.06);

      const fillG = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, baseY-amp*0.9, 0, bottomY);
      fillG.addColorStop(0.00, rgbStr(c0, 1));
      fillG.addColorStop(0.55, rgbStr(c1, 1));
      fillG.addColorStop(1.00, rgbStr(c2, 1));

      // 山體剪影填色
      ctx.save();
      ctx.globalAlpha = G.fillAlpha * alpha;
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(0, bottomY);
      ctx.lineTo(pts[0][0], pts[0][1]);
      for(let k=1;k<pts.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(pts[k][0], pts[k][1]);
      ctx.lineTo(W, bottomY);
      ctx.closePath();
      ctx.fillStyle = fillG;
      ctx.fill();
      ctx.restore();

      // 柔光邊緣（遠更柔、近略收）
      const edgeA = (G.edgeGlow + 0.06*(1-t)) * alpha;
      const edgeW = lerp(G.edgeWidthFar, G.edgeWidthNear, t);

      ctx.save();
      ctx.globalAlpha = edgeA;
      ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(lighten(c1, 0.28), 1);
      ctx.lineWidth = edgeW;
      ctx.lineJoin="round"; ctx.lineCap="round";
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(pts[0][0], pts[0][1]);
      for(let k=1;k<pts.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(pts[k][0], pts[k][1]);
      ctx.stroke();
      ctx.restore();

      // 薄邊線（讓層次更清楚）
      ctx.save();
      ctx.globalAlpha = (0.08 + 0.10*(1-t)) * alpha;
      ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(lighten(c0, 0.35), 1);
      ctx.lineWidth = lerp(1.2, 2.2, 1-t);
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(pts[0][0], pts[0][1]);
      for(let k=1;k<pts.length;k++) ctx.lineTo(pts[k][0], pts[k][1]);
      ctx.stroke();
      ctx.restore();
    }

    // 暗角（夜晚更明顯）
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(
      W*0.5, H*0.42, Math.min(W,H)*0.18,
      W*0.5, H*0.5,  Math.min(W,H)*0.95
    );
    vig.addColorStop(0, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    vig.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,${(0.12 + 0.44*night)*alpha})`);
    ctx.fillStyle = vig;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    // 底部霧（像你參考圖那種白霧漸層）
    const fog = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, H*0.68, 0, H*1.02);
    fog.addColorStop(0, `rgba(255,255,255,0)`);
    fog.addColorStop(1, `rgba(255,255,255,${0.58*alpha})`);
    ctx.fillStyle = fog;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  }

  // ---------- Corridor ----------
  function drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, flow, moveStrength, sky, alpha=1){
    const topY = sunY + Math.min(W,H)*0.04;
    const botY = H*1.02;

    const topW = W*0.12;
    const botW = W*0.90;
    const cx = sunX;

    const baseA = mixRGB([140,240,255],[255,84,214],0.25);
    const baseB = mixRGB([60,120,255],[0,0,0],0.08);

    const grd = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, topY, 0, botY);
    grd.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(mixRGB(baseA, sky, 0.18), 0.50*alpha));
    grd.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(mixRGB(baseB, sky, 0.12), 0.88*alpha));

    const x1t = cx - topW*0.5, x2t = cx + topW*0.5;
    const x1b = cx - botW*0.5, x2b = cx + botW*0.5;

    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(x1t, topY); ctx.lineTo(x2t, topY);
    ctx.lineTo(x2b, botY); ctx.lineTo(x1b, botY);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.clip();

    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.84;
    ctx.fillStyle = grd;
    ctx.fillRect(0, topY, W, botY-topY);

    // stripe 隨前進加速（按住更強）
    const speed = lerp(0.0, 1.0, moveStrength);
    const stripeOffset = (flow * 260 * (0.15 + 0.85*speed)) % 96;

    for(let i=-4;i<30;i++){
      const y = topY + i*34 + stripeOffset;
      const t = clamp((y-topY)/(botY-topY),0,1);
      const halfW = lerp(topW*0.55, botW*0.55, smooth(t));
      const xl = cx-halfW, xr=cx+halfW;

      const cfg = STATE.ridges[(i+100)%STATE.ridges.length];
      const col = hexToRgb(cfg.stops[1]);
      const stripeCol = mixRGB([255,255,255], col, 0.30);

      const a = lerp(0.26, 0.06, t) * alpha;
      ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(stripeCol, a);
      ctx.lineWidth = lerp(1.8, 1.0, t);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(xl,y); ctx.lineTo(xr,y); ctx.stroke();
    }

    ctx.restore();

    // 洞口感
    const holeR = Math.min(W,H)*0.22;
    const hole = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, topY, 0, cx, topY, holeR);
    hole.addColorStop(0, `rgba(16,14,22,${0.58*alpha})`);
    hole.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle = hole;
    ctx.fillRect(cx-holeR, topY-holeR, holeR*2, holeR*2);
  }

  // ---------- Sun (永遠最後畫) ----------
  function drawSun(x,y,r,color,glow=1,alpha=1){
    const R = r*(7*glow);
    const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
    g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(color, 0.26*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(0.22, rgbStr(lighten(color,0.10), 0.16*alpha));
    g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(color, 0.98*alpha); ctx.fill();

    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x-r*0.22,y-r*0.22,r*0.35,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${0.36*alpha})`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // ---------- Layer 3: Space ----------
  function drawSpace(alpha=1){
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(5,6,12,${alpha})`;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    const neb=ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.35,H*0.35,0, W*0.35,H*0.35, Math.min(W,H)*0.9);
    neb.addColorStop(0, `rgba(120,90,255,${0.10*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(0.5, `rgba(80,220,255,${0.05*alpha})`);
    neb.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
    ctx.fillStyle=neb;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

    for(let i=0;i<140;i++){
      const x=(hash2(i,9.1)*W), y=(hash2(i,2.7)*H);
      const a=(hash2(i,6.3)*0.06+0.01)*alpha;
      const r=hash2(i,4.2)*1.2+0.2;
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }

    for(const s of stars){
      const x=s.x*W, y=s.y*H;
      const tw=(Math.sin(time*1.6+s.twSeed)*0.5+0.5);
      const a=lerp(0.35,0.95,tw)*alpha;

      const R=s.r*10;
      const g=ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,R);
      g.addColorStop(0, rgbStr(s.color, 0.24*a));
      g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
      ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(x-R,y-R,R*2,R*2);

      ctx.fillStyle=rgbStr(s.color,a);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,s.r,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
    }
  }

  // ---------- Update / Render ----------
  function update(dt){
    time += dt;

    // 1) 山河永遠流動
    ambientFlow += dt * STATE.global.ambientFlowSpeed;

    // 2) 滾輪縮放
    zoomVel *= 0.84;
    zoom = clamp(zoom - zoomVel, 0, 1);

    // 3) 日夜往返（不瞬跳）
    timeDay = (timeDay + dt*0.05) % 2;           // 0..2
    dayPhase = timeDay <= 1 ? timeDay : (2 - timeDay); // 0..1..0
    const sky = skyAt(dayPhase);

    const inTerrain = (zoom > 0.45);
    const wantsMove = pointer.down && !inColorize && inTerrain;

    // 4) 前進只影響 travel（按住才加速）
    const targetVel = wantsMove ? 1 : 0;
    travelVel += (targetVel - travelVel) * (1 - Math.pow(0.001, dt));
    travel += travelVel * dt * 1.55;

    // 5) 抵達亮點 → 染色 → 記星
    if(!inColorize){
      if(wantsMove) reach -= dt*0.62;
      else          reach += dt*0.08;
      reach = clamp(reach,0,1);

      if(reach <= 0.04){
        inColorize=true;
        colorizeT=0;
        pendingColor=randomDreamColor();
      }
    } else {
      colorizeT += dt*1.15;
      if(colorizeT >= 1){
        addStar(pendingColor);
        sun.curColor = sun.baseColor.slice();
        inColorize=false;
        reach=1;
      } else {
        const t=colorizeT;
        const up = t<0.55 ? smooth(t/0.55) : smooth((1-t)/0.45);
        sun.curColor = mixRGB(sun.baseColor, pendingColor, up);
      }
    }

    render(sky);
  }

  function render(sky){
    const layer = currentLayer();
    const terrainAlpha = clamp((zoom - 0.35)/0.65, 0, 1);
    const spaceAlpha = 1 - terrainAlpha;

    if(spaceAlpha>0.001) drawSpace(spaceAlpha);

    if(terrainAlpha>0.001){
      // 山河：永遠流動 + 按住時額外加速（可設 travelFlowBoost=0）
      const terrainFlow = ambientFlow + travel * STATE.global.travelFlowBoost;

      drawMultiRidgeTerrainSilhouette(sky, terrainFlow, terrainAlpha);

      const sunX = W*(sun.x + Math.sin(time*0.20)*0.002);
      const sunY = H*(sun.y + Math.cos(time*0.16)*0.002);

      // 通道：仍然主要跟「前進 travel」連動（按住才更有前進感）
      drawCorridor(sunX, sunY, travel, travelVel, sky, terrainAlpha);

      // 第二層染色效果
      if(inColorize){
        const t=smooth(colorizeT);
        const flashA = lerp(0.00,0.30, Math.sin(Math.PI*t));
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${flashA*terrainAlpha})`;
        ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

        const baseR = Math.min(W,H)*0.018;
        const ringR = lerp(baseR*2.2, Math.min(W,H)*0.36, t);
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(sunX,sunY,ringR,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.strokeStyle = rgbStr(pendingColor, 0.48*terrainAlpha);
        ctx.lineWidth = lerp(2.8,1.0,t);
        ctx.stroke();
      }

      // 亮點：永遠最後畫，保證可見；按住前進時變大靠近
      const baseR = Math.min(W,H)*0.018;
      const grow = lerp(1.0, 3.1, smooth(1-reach));
      const pulse = (Math.sin(time*1.2)*0.5+0.5);
      const glow  = lerp(1.0, 2.1, smooth(1-reach));
      drawSun(sunX, sunY, baseR*grow*(1.0+pulse*0.05), sun.curColor, glow, terrainAlpha);

      // 提示
      if(!pointer.down && !inColorize){
        const a=(Math.sin(time*2.0)*0.5+0.5)*0.25*terrainAlpha;
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,${a})`;
        ctx.font=`600 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.018))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
        ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
        ctx.fillText('按住左鍵追光前進', W*0.5, H*0.82);
      }
    }

    // HUD
    if(pillLayer){
      pillLayer.textContent = `layer: ${inColorize ? '2' : layer}`;
      pillStars.textContent = `stars: ${stars.length}`;
      pillZoom.textContent  = `zoom: ${zoom.toFixed(2)}`;
      pillTime.textContent  = `time: ${Math.round(dayPhase*100)}%`;
    }

    if(layer===3 && !inColorize){
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.55)`;
      ctx.font=`500 ${Math.max(12, Math.floor(Math.min(W,H)*0.016))}px ui-sans-serif, system-ui`;
      ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
      ctx.fillText('滾輪放大回到地勢圖（第一層）', W*0.5, H*0.90);
      if(stars.length===0){
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(255,255,255,0.42)`;
        ctx.fillText('宇宙尚未生成繁星：先回去追光並完成染色', W*0.5, H*0.84);
      }
    }
  }

  // ---------- Loop ----------
  let last=performance.now();
  function loop(now){
    const dt=Math.min(0.033,(now-last)/1000);
    last=now;
    update(dt);
    requestAnimationFrame(loop);
  }
  requestAnimationFrame(loop);
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
你接下來最可能想調的兩個地方

山永遠流動速度：STATE.global.ambientFlowSpeed

按住前進時山也加速多少：STATE.global.travelFlowBoost（不想影響就設 0）

如果你想讓疊片更像你圖裡「左側更高、右側也更高，中間通道更乾淨」，我可以再把 valley mask 做得更可控（例如加 valleyWidth / valleyStrength 兩個參數）。



你說：

如果你想讓疊片更像你圖裡「左側更高、右側也更高，中間通道更乾淨」，我可以再把 valley mask 做得更可控（例如加 `valleyWidth / valleyStrength` 兩個參數）。

已上傳一個圖像
好 你做
另外，中間的那條道路要怎麼修改顏色透明度那些？還有最下面也要蓋一層薄霧


ChatGPT 說：

好，我來「做」：我會把 中間通道更乾淨 做成可控參數（valleyWidth / valleyStrength），並且把你問的：

道路顏色/透明度

最下面再蓋一層薄霧

都做成「後台可調」的參數（不出 UI）。

下面給你 直接貼上就會生效的改動（不用重打一整份 HTML，但你照著改就完成）。

1) 先在 STATE.global 加上道路與 valley、薄霧參數

在你現有的 STATE.global 裡面（你有 ambientFlowSpeed / travelFlowBoost 那區），加上這段：

JavaScript
// —— 通道（道路）外觀 —— 
corridor: {
  alpha: 0.82,          // 通道整體透明度（0~1）
  topAlpha: 0.52,       // 通道上端透明度（靠洞口）
  bottomAlpha: 0.90,    // 通道下端透明度（靠鏡頭）
  colorA: "#7fe8ff",    // 通道上端色（偏亮）
  colorB: "#1e6bff",    // 通道下端色（偏深）
  mixWithSky: 0.18,     // 跟天空混色（0~0.4 推薦）
  stripeAlpha: 0.26,    // 通道條紋透明度
  stripeSpacing: 34,    // 條紋間距
  stripeSpeed: 260      // 條紋速度（前進時更明顯）
},

// —— 中央 valley（讓中間更空、兩側更高）——
valley: {
  strength: 0.55,   // 0=沒效果；越大中間越乾淨、兩側越抬高（0.3~0.9）
  width: 0.26       // 中間乾淨區寬度（0.18~0.40）
},

// —— 底部薄霧（在你圈的最下面再蓋一層）——
bottomMist: {
  startY: 0.80,     // 霧從畫面高度的哪裡開始（0~1）
  endY: 1.02,       // 霧到哪裡結束（可超過1）
  alpha: 0.35       // 薄霧強度
}
2) 讓「中間通道更乾淨」：更新 valley mask（已可調）

到你的 drawMultiRidgeTerrainSilhouette(...) 裡，找到這段（我之前有寫）：

JavaScript
const mid = x/W - 0.5;
const valley = 1 - Math.exp(-(mid*mid)/0.05);
const sideBoost = lerp(0.85, 1.35, valley);

把它整段換成下面這段（用你剛加的參數）：

JavaScript
const mid = (x / W) - 0.5;

// width 控制中間乾淨區寬度；strength 控制兩側抬高程度
const vw = STATE.global.valley.width;          // 0.18~0.40
const vs = STATE.global.valley.strength;       // 0~0.9

// 讓中間接近 0、兩側接近 1 的權重
const valley = 1 - Math.exp(-(mid*mid) / (vw*vw));
const sideBoost = 1 + valley * vs;             // 1~(1+vs)

這樣你要中間更空，就把 strength 拉高、或 width 拉大。

3) 道路顏色/透明度怎麼改：更新 drawCorridor(...) 用剛剛的設定

找到 drawCorridor(...) 裡面這段（你現在有 baseA/baseB + grd 的寫法），把計算顏色/透明度那段改成下面這樣（保留其餘 clip、stripe 的程式）：

把這段：

grd.addColorStop(1, rgbStr(bMix, C.bottomAlpha * C.alpha * alpha));

然後在畫條紋那段，找到：

JavaScript

以及把 stripeSpacing、stripeSpeed 套用（你原本是固定 34、260）：

換成：

JavaScript

② 把 skyAt() 換成這個版本

找到你現在的：

JavaScript
function skyAt(t){ ... }

改成：

JavaScript
function skyAt(t){
  const cycle = STATE.dayCycle;

  // 找到區間
  for(let i=0;i<cycle.length-1;i++){
    const a = cycle[i];
    const b = cycle[i+1];

    if(t >= a.t && t <= b.t){
      const localT = (t - a.t) / (b.t - a.t);
      return mixRGB(
        hexToRgb(a.color),
        hexToRgb(b.color),
        smooth(localT)
      );
    }
  }

  return hexToRgb(cycle[cycle.length-1].color);
}
🔥 這樣你可以做什麼？

  { t: 0.40, color: "#ffc36f" },   // 橘
  { t: 0.60, color: "#4fc3ff" },   // 藍
  { t: 0.80, color: "#0d0d15" },   // 夜
  { t: 1.00, color: "#ffffff" }
]

或者更夢核一點：

ChatGPT 說：

我懂你說的「黑黑的暈影一直在」是什麼：
現在你的光暈其實是用 radialGradient 畫一張方形 fillRect，再加上你整體場景裡還有 暗角 vignette / 洞口陰影 hole，所以就算光暈是白色，周圍仍然會被「黑色漸層」壓住，看起來像一圈黑暈。

我直接給你 最乾淨的修法：
✅ 光暈改成 screen / lighter 的加亮模式（只會加亮，不會加黑）
✅ 光暈只畫在 圓形範圍（不再用 fillRect 擴散整塊）
✅ 把洞口陰影（hole）在靠近太陽的地方弱化（避免黑暈蓋上去）

1) 直接把 drawSun() 整段替換成這個（最推薦）
JavaScript
function drawSun(x,y,r,color,glow=1,alpha=1){
  // —— 可調：光暈顏色 / 強度 / 範圍 ——
  const glowColor = hexToRgb("#ffffff");    // 你要的光暈色
  const glowSize = 10;                      // 光暈半徑倍率（越大越擴散）
  const glowA0 = 0.55;                      // 中心光暈透明度
  const glowA1 = 0.18;                      // 中段光暈透明度

  const R = r * (glowSize * glow);

  // 1) 光暈：用「加亮」混合模式，避免任何黑暈
  ctx.save();
  ctx.globalCompositeOperation = "screen";  // 只加亮
  ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;

  const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(x,y,0, x,y,R);
  g.addColorStop(0.00, rgbStr(glowColor, glowA0));
  g.addColorStop(0.18, rgbStr(glowColor, glowA1));
  g.addColorStop(1.00, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);

  // 不用 fillRect，改用圓形填滿（避免方形影子感）
  ctx.fillStyle = g;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(x,y,R,0,Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.restore();

  // 2) 本體（不加亮模式，正常畫）
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle = rgbStr(color, 0.98*alpha);
  ctx.fill();

  // 3) 高光
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(x-r*0.22,y-r*0.22,r*0.35,0,Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${0.36*alpha})`;
  ctx.fill();
}

這樣做完：光暈只會「疊亮」，不可能出現黑暈。

2) 你畫面那圈「黑影」多半也來自洞口陰影（hole）

在 drawCorridor() 裡你有這段（洞口感）：

JavaScript
const hole = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, topY, 0, cx, topY, holeR);
hole.addColorStop(0, `rgba(16,14,22,${0.58*alpha})`);
hole.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,0)`);
ctx.fillStyle = hole;
ctx.fillRect(cx-holeR, topY-holeR, holeR*2, holeR*2);

把中心那個 0.58 改小一點，例如：

JavaScript
hole.addColorStop(0, `rgba(16,14,22,${0.28*alpha})`);

這樣洞口不會一直把太陽周圍壓黑。

3) 如果你還想「完全不要任何暗角」

在 drawMultiRidgeTerrainSilhouette() 裡有 vignette（暗角）。
你想讓光點附近永遠乾淨，可以把暗角強度降一半：

JavaScript
vig.addColorStop(1, `rgba(0,0,0,${(0.06 + 0.22*night)*alpha})`);

（原本是 0.12 + 0.44*night 那種程度）

你先做最關鍵的兩步就會改善 90%

換掉 drawSun()（screen + 圓形光暈）

把 hole 中心 alpha 0.58 → 0.28
